Both wrapped in try/except so a missing migration just zeroes the field instead of 500-ing the entire hub.

### Delve overhaul phase 3: class craftables, quests, achievements
- **Crafting catalog gains 11 class-themed recipes**. `arrow_bundle_craft` + `broadhead_bundle_craft` (fletching) cover bow ammo; `bolt_bundle_craft` + `piercing_bolts_craft` (smithing) cover crossbow ammo; `scroll_volley_inscribe` + `scroll_mark_target_inscribe` (enchanting) cover archer scrolls; `thorn_aura_brew_craft` + `wildshape_potion_craft` + `regrowth_brew_craft` (alchemy) cover druid brews; `mana_draught_distill` + `scroll_sanctuary_inscribe` cover mage utility. Each routes to its `consum/*` apply target so the consumable stack tops up the right inventory column without crafting needing class awareness.
- **Class-aware bus events**. `services.dungeon` + `cogs.dungeon` now fan out per-class trigger names alongside the existing generic ones: `delve_kill_<class>`, `delve_capture_<class>`, `delve_skill_<skill_key>` (volley, wildshape, fireball, cleave, backstab), `delve_class_picked` + `delve_class_picked_<class>`, `delve_class_lv10_<class>`, `delve_stat_spent`, `craft_ammo`. Quests + achievements key off these directly so per-class progression counts cleanly without a new payload-aware filter mechanic.
- **6 new daily / weekly quests**. Daily: Loose A Volley (3x Volley), Wild At Heart (3x Wildshape), Quiver Stocked (5x ammo crafts), Sharpen Up (any stat point spent), Reinvent Yourself (any class reroll). Weekly: Marksman (25 kills as Archer), Speak To The Wild (3 captures as Druid).
- **9 new achievements**. Apprentice Archer + Apprentice Druid (first class pick); Volley Master (25 volleys) + Beast Speaker (25 wildshapes); Min-Maxer (50 total stat points spent); Class Chameleon + Identity Crisis (1 + 5 rerolls); Iron Veteran / Channeler / Shadowstep / Sharpshooter / Forest Walker (Lv. 10 in each respective class).

### Delve overhaul phase 2: ranged combat, class skills, stat-point spending
- **Ranged vs melee combat split**. `services.dungeon.resolve_attack` was a single SPD-tied turn-order loop; now it branches on the equipped weapon's `attack_kind`. Ranged weapons (bow / crossbow) take their first swing **before** the mob regardless of SPD (kiting), get +5% crit on the opener, and the mob's counter-swing in the same round only deals 85% damage (`RANGED_RETALIATION_MULT`). Melee combat keeps the legacy SPD-tie behavior.
- **Ammo system**. Bow weapons consume one `arrow_bundle` per swing (3 for Volley). Crossbows pull from `bolt_bundle` the same way. Out-of-ammo ranged shots auto-fall back to 50% damage (`OUT_OF_AMMO_DAMAGE_MULT`) so running dry is a soft tax, not a hard lockout. New ammo variants (`broadhead_bundle`, `piercing_bolts`) bump per-shot damage by 25-30% via `ammo_dmg_mult`. Direct `,delve use arrow_bundle` is rejected -- ammo only feeds the weapon during a swing.
- **Volley (Archer)** and **Wildshape (Druid)** class skills. Volley = 3 arrow swings at 0.7x each + bonus crit (~2.1x effective with crit upside, burns 3 ammo). Wildshape = single 2.0x beast-strike that heals 15% max HP. Both routed through `resolve_attack`'s `mode='skill'` branch with their own ammo/regen logic.
- **New buff / regen / skill_reset consumable kinds**. `scroll_volley` (charges next basic ranged attack to 3 shots), `scroll_mark_target` (next 3 attacks auto-crit), `thorn_aura_brew` (reflect 30% melee dmg for 4 rounds), `wildshape_potion` (+50% ATK + heal 5% HP/turn for 3 rounds), `regrowth_brew` (+10% HP/turn for 5 rounds), `mana_draught` (resets class-skill cooldown), `scroll_sanctuary` (halve incoming damage for 2 rounds). Buffs persist across rooms via the new `player_buffs` JSONB column on `user_dungeon` (migration `0191`), tick down per combat round, and stack only by overwriting with the longer remaining duration.
- **Stat-point spending lives in `,delve upgrade`**. Mirrors `,buddy upgrade`: 4 lanes (Hardiness +4 max HP, Power +0.6 ATK, Vigor +0.005 SPD, Wisdom +0.6 INT) with sticky allocation across reroll / equip / run lifecycle. INT is folded into spell-skill damage (`Fireball`, `Wildshape`) so Mage / Druid have a meaningful spend lane. Hardiness ALSO bumps current HP by the same delta on spend so allocating mid-rest doesn't leave you missing health.
- **`,delve reroll <class>` ships**. Geometric cost (`5,000 USD * 2^N`), 6-hour cooldown gated DB-side via `EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (NOW() - last_class_reroll_at))`. Refused mid-run; preserves level / XP / captures / inventory / stat-point allocations; snaps the new class's starter weapon + armor into the inventory and equips them. A Vigor-stacked Rogue can carry that build cleanly to Archer.
- **Spell skills now read INT**. Mage Fireball + Druid Wildshape damage adds `INT * 1.2` on top of base ATK so the Wisdom investment shows up in actual swing damage rather than being decorative. Physical skills (Cleave / Backstab / Volley) keep their pure-ATK math.

### Delve overhaul phase 1: archer, druid, weapon/armor types, stat points
- **Two new delve classes**. `,delve class archer` and `,delve class druid` now ship alongside warrior / mage / rogue, each with their own combat profile, weapon restriction, and starter kit. Archers run Bow / Crossbow + medium leather; Druids channel Rod + light robes; Warriors stay sword/axe/mace + heavy plate; Mages stay Staff + light robes; Rogues stay Shortsword + medium leather. Migration `0190` widens the `user_dungeon.class_chk` constraint so the new classes can be persisted.
- **Weapon + armor type taxonomy**. Every entry in `WEAPONS` is tagged with `weapon_type` (`longsword/shortsword/axe/mace/bow/crossbow/staff/rod`) and `attack_kind` (`melee/ranged`). Every entry in `ARMOR` is tagged with `armor_type` (`light/medium/heavy`). `services.dungeon.equip_item` now refuses class-incompatible gear with a human-readable hint (`"A Mage can't wear Plate Armor (heavy armor). Allowed: light."`). No more accidentally equipping a mythril plate as an Archer.
- **New gear catalog**. 8 bows, 5 crossbows, 8 staves, 7 rods, plus 7 light robes and 8 medium hides spanning tiers 0-11 (apprentice through endgame). The fee curve mirrors the existing sword line so cross-class economy stays balanced -- e.g. an Archer's tier-5 elven longbow runs the same RUNE as a Warrior's mythril sword.
- **Stat-point allocation now lives on `user_dungeon`**. New columns `hp_alloc / atk_alloc / spd_alloc / int_alloc` mirror the buddy upgrade system. Each delve level grants `STAT_POINTS_PER_LEVEL = 1` point; per-point payoffs are `+4 max HP / +0.6 ATK / +0.005 SPD / +0.6 INT` (INT scales spell damage so caster classes have something to spend on). Phase 2 wires the upgrade UI; this commit just lays the schema + helper.
- **Class reroll plumbing**. `class_rerolls_used` + `last_class_reroll_at` columns added with a CHECK + `class_reroll_cost_usd(n) = 5,000 USD * 2^n` helper. Phase 3 ships the user-facing `,delve reroll <class>` command.
- **`,delve class` lists allowed weapons / armor per class**. The error embed players see when they typo a class name now lists each class's `weapon_types` + `armor_types` so they can make an informed pick.
- **Starter kit auto-mints into the inventory on class pick**. `set_class` now stamps the class's `starter_weapon` + `starter_armor` into both `equipped_*` and the `weapons_owned/armor_owned` JSONB so newly picked classes can immediately fight without buying anything.

### Buddy panel + shelter clarity pass
- **Shelter listing surfaces rarity**. `,buddy shelter` rows previously showed only `#id  emoji  Name  -  Lv. N  -  reason`, so a Common adoption looked identical to a Legendary one and players had to adopt blind to find out. Each row now reads `#id  emoji  **Name**  -  **<Rarity>** Lv. N  -  reason` with the rarity name pulled from `buddies_config.rarity_meta`, matching how rarity is displayed everywhere else (panel header, AH listings, battle results). `services/buddy_lifecycle.list_shelter` was widened to also fetch `rarity_tier` so the cog can render this without a second round-trip.
- **Buddy panel folds upgrades into the visible combat stats**. `,buddy` previously displayed HP / ATK / SPD computed from `tier_meta + level + mood` ONLY -- the player's spent stat points (`hp_alloc / atk_alloc / spd_alloc`, allocated via `,buddy upgrade`) were silently ignored on the panel even though `services.buddy_battle.Fighter.from_row` applied them in actual fights. The panel now mirrors the Fighter formula exactly so the numbers can no longer disagree with battles.
- **Per-stat upgrade tag on the Combat line**. Each upgraded stat picks up an `*(+N upg)*` tag so players can see at a glance how much of their displayed HP / ATK / SPD comes from spent points vs base + level + tier + mood.
- **New `Upgrades` panel field**. Lists Hardiness / Power / Vigor allocations with the converted bonus (`+12 max HP`, `+1.5 ATK`, `+0.025 SPD`), the per-point conversion rate as a footnote (so "+3 HP / +0.5 ATK / +0.5% SPD per point") and the running total spent. When the player has unspent points it surfaces them prominently with a hint to run `,buddy upgrade`, so points stop sitting unallocated because the panel never reminded them.
- **Battle challenge / result blocks also reflect upgrades**. `_fighter_field` was on the same stale formula so the prompt embed for `,buddy battle` would understate a heavily upgraded buddy's stats. Now matches the Fighter exactly too -- challenge previews can no longer mislead either fighter about what they're walking into.

### Fishing: dynamic hook window + secondary REEL action
- **Hook window scales per cast.** Was a flat `HOOK_WINDOW_S = 3.0s` for everyone. New `fishing_config.compute_hook_window(rod_tier, fish_level, zone_tier, rarity_tier)` returns a per-cast deadline:
  - **Rod tier**: +6% per tier (better gear = more time)
  - **Fishing level**: +1.5% per level (mastery widens the window)
  - **Zone tier**: −8% per tier above 1 (deeper zones are chaotic)
  - **Rarity tier**: −12.5% per tier above 1 (legendary fish are tighter); cog passes the bucket-rarity hint when available
  - **Random jitter**: ±15% so streaks don't feel mechanical
  - Floor 1.2s, ceiling 6.0s
- **Secondary mid-cast REEL action.** New `fc.SECONDARY_TRIGGER_CHANCE = 0.25` so ~1 in 4 casts inserts a `🌀 PULL!` prompt before the bite frame. Players have `fc.SECONDARY_WINDOW_S = 2.0s` to click `REEL!`. If the prompt fires and the player misses → catch is forced to a miss outcome (fish slips). If they hit:
  - **Sweet hook + secondary** → 2.0× quality bonus (legendary catch territory)
  - **Secondary only (no sweet)** → 1.5× bonus (matches the legacy sweet bonus, so missing the sweet but nailing the secondary still pays off)
- **`services/fishing.py:cast_resolve`** now accepts `hook_window_s`, `secondary_required`, `secondary_hit` kwargs. Quality gating compares against the actual presented window (not the constant) so the player can never be "late" against a deadline they didn't see. `CastView` stamps the per-cast window at bite time, runs the secondary prompt when triggered, and forwards both into the resolver.
- Backwards-compatible: legacy callers (force-miss path on view abort, `WildBattleView` exit, etc.) still work with the new signature. `_on_reel` callback acknowledges within Discord's 3s budget; window-mismatch races are rejected by an explicit elapsed-time check.

### `,buddy species` interactive roster
- **Type-filter dropdown.** Was a flat embed listing every species grouped by rarity. Now it's an interactive panel with a row-0 dropdown: `All Species / Forest Affinity / Reef Affinity / Mine Affinity / Ruins Affinity / Neutral`. Affinity comes from `expeditions_config.SPECIES_AFFINITY` so the same buckets that drive expedition loot bonuses now drive species browsing too.
- **Per-species detail.** Each row shows hatch %, affinity tag, every signature lane the (species, rarity-tier) buffs (`Buffs: Chat XP · Work payout · Fishing yield`), the species ability + description, and base HP/ATK pulled from the rarity tier's combat stats. Players evaluating a species choice for a destination / lane have the full picture in one place instead of cross-referencing `,db` + `,buddy stats` + `,expedition help`.
- Selecting an affinity also surfaces the destination blurb (`Quiet, dappled, full of curious herbs.` etc.) plus the +25% loot reminder so the link between species choice and expedition payoff is explicit.

### `,items` per-token picker + visible token IDs
- **Pick-a-specific-token dropdown on the `,items` overview.** Player feedback: "make individual items in a stack selectable, so if I want to use a particular egg or a particular fish I can send / use / list it individually. Also need to add the token id to items list -- I can't even see it to transfer or sell or list anything." New `_TokenPickSelect` on row 3 lists up to 25 of the player's owned tokens (filtered by the current kind selection), each option formatted with metadata-rich copy so the player can pick the SPECIFIC token they want:
  - Fish: `Trout - 4.2 lbs  ·  lur:abc12`
  - Egg: `Wecco Egg - Rare  ·  bud:xyz98`
  - Buddy: `Sparky L12  ·  bud:def45`
  - Generic: `Worm Bait  ·  lur:abc34`
- Selection opens an ephemeral inspect embed (token id, contract, network, status, metadata) plus the standard `TokenActionView` (List on AH / Transfer / View Contract / Refresh) so every per-token action is one click away from the overview. No need to type the token id manually.
- Picker rebuilds on every refresh / kind-switch / sort cycle so newly minted / sold / gifted tokens stay in sync. Initial paint also populates the dropdown so it's available before the first interaction.
- Footer copy on the overview embed updated to point players at the new dropdown ("Pick a specific token (row 3) to inspect / list / transfer").

### Capture is now an option on every wild encounter
- **`Try Capture` button on shelter-escape (`,buddy` escape event) prompts.** `_EscapedBuddyView` previously offered only `⚔️ Challenge`. New button does a one-shot 20% capture roll with no fight: success flips the escaped buddy to `'owned'` under the clicker (same path as the Challenge-then-win flow); failure dismisses the encounter with the buddy returning to the shelter for normal `,buddy shelter` adoption. Shelter-cap honoured.
- **`Try Capture` on fishing wild encounters.** `cogs/fishing.py:_WildBattleView` got the same button alongside Challenge. Routes through `services.fishing.resolve_wild_battle(won=True/False)` so the cc_buddies insert + LURE/REEL/BBT credit + counter bumps + bus events all run through the canonical resolver -- no risk of the manual capture bypassing analytics.
- Same 20% chance (`fishing_config.WILD_BATTLE_CAPTURE_CHANCE` / hard-coded for the buddy escape path) as the existing post-fight auto-capture roll, so the affordance doesn't trivialise wild battles. Players who want a guaranteed catch still click Challenge and fight to weaken the wild buddy.
- Delve and farm wild battles already had a Capture button (delve gates on enemy HP < threshold mid-fight; farm grants on win). Unchanged.

### AH listings now decrement / restore JSONB inventory too
- **`,ah list <name>` removes the item from your per-cog inventory.** Pre-fix the token-path AH list flow only escrowed the NFT (`item_instances.owner_user_id = NULL`); the parallel JSONB count on `user_fishing.fish_inventory` / `user_farming.crops_inventory` / etc. stayed put, so listing a fish still showed it in `,fish inv`. `services/auction.py:create_listing_by_token` now ALSO calls the matching `_LOCK_HANDLERS[kind]` for fish / crop / ore / weapon / armor / consumable / crafted right after the NFT escrow, inside the same `db.atomic()` block. Wrapped in try/except so a missing JSONB row (NFT minted via expedition / backfill with no JSONB entry) doesn't roll back the listing.
- **`,ah cancel` restores the inventory.** `cancel_listing` token-path now mirrors the lock with `_RETURN_HANDLERS[kind]` for the same set of kinds. Cancelling a listing puts the item back in `,fish inv` / `,farm inv` / etc. alongside the NFT sweep back to the seller.
- **`,ah buy` deposits to the buyer's inventory.** `buy_listing` token-path now calls `_DELIVER_HANDLERS[kind]` so the buyer sees their purchase in their per-cog inventory immediately, not just in `,items`. Same try/except envelope for safety -- the NFT transfer already moved ownership at the source-of-truth layer.
- Bait / junk / shop / stone are unchanged here -- those kinds are NFT-only with no JSONB count to sync.

### Buddy panel dropdown stops desyncing on the live tick
- **Live tick no longer rebuilds `_BuddySelect` mid-session.** Every minute or so the buddy panel's live tick fires `_get_data` to re-fetch state for the ASCII frame; pre-fix that path also called `view._rebuild_buddy_select(live_pages)`, which removed the active select from `self.children` and replaced it with a fresh instance. The tick then ran `await msg.edit(embed=rendered)` -- embed only, the view was never pushed to Discord. Discord's display kept the OLD select component while the in-memory view tracked a new (different) one. The next dropdown click landed at discord.py with no matching child to route to: `View interaction referencing unknown view for item <_BuddySelect ... id=14>. Discarding` plus `"this interaction failed"` for the player. Buttons (which never get rebuilt) kept working, which is why the user reported "broken with the dropdown but not with arrow keys."
- The select is still rebuilt on the explicit `_redraw` path (Prev/Next/Set Active button clicks, the dropdown's own callback, and the initial render) -- those paths all call `interaction.response.edit_message(view=self)` (or `ctx.reply(view=self)` on first render) which pushes the updated component list to Discord. Embed-only live-tick edits stop touching the children.

### Buddy panel survives bot restarts (no more "this interaction failed")
- **`BuddyPanelView` is now a persistent view.** Pre-fix every bot restart wiped the in-memory view registry, so any panel opened in the previous session produced "View interaction referencing unknown view for item ... Discarding" + Discord's generic "this interaction failed" on every click. Now: `timeout=None`, every button + the row-3 buddy select carries an explicit `custom_id` (`buddy_panel:feed`, `:pet`, `:talk`, `:rename`, `:refresh`, `:list_ah`, `:prev`, `:next`, `:set_active`, `:select`), and `Buddy.cog_load` registers a stub view via `bot.add_view(BuddyPanelView())` so post-restart interactions route to it cleanly.
- The persistent stub's `interaction_check` detects the no-args rehydrated state and short-circuits with an ephemeral `"This buddy panel was opened in a previous session and has expired. Run ,buddy to open a fresh one."` hint. Live in-memory views still gate on `interaction.user.id == self.owner_id` exactly like before.
- The stub also instantiates a placeholder `_BuddySelect` with empty options at registration time so the dropdown's custom_id matches in discord.py's persistent-view routing -- without that, dropdown clicks on stale panels would still fall through unmatched. The placeholder never sees a real callback (interaction_check rejects every click on the stub).

### `,buddy species` surfaces the new rarity-extra lanes
- **Per-rarity lane breakdown on the species list.** Player feedback: "where do I see the new buddy passives? They aren't showing on buddy embeds or species list or anywhere." The `,buddy` panel got a `✨ Passive effects` field in the cross-cog passives commit (`05b51c2`) but the `,buddy species` roster command was untouched. Each rarity header now appends `+N extra signature lane(s)` so players see at a glance what their tier unlocks; each species row gets a muted `Buffs: <lane>, <lane>, ...` line listing every signature lane the (species, tier) combo buffs at the fast ramp -- pulled straight from `buddy_bonus_lanes_for(species, tier)` so the display matches the actual multiplier wiring.
- The original ASCII-panel field (`✨ Passive effects` on `,buddy stats`) is unchanged and still renders for any (species, tier) combo with a known `bonus_lane`. If the field doesn't appear, force a panel re-open with `,buddy` -- live-tick views from before the cross-cog commit don't always pick up new fields until the message is replaced.

### Bug fixes from new prod logs
- **`,admin buddy spawn` no longer trips `cc_buddies_status_chk`.** Migration `0169_cc_buddies_storage_status.sql` rewrote the status CHECK as `('owned', 'shelter', 'stored')` -- which dropped `'escaped'` (added by 0121) AND never included `'auction'` (added by my buddy AH listing flow). Both states are written by live code (`services.buddy_world.mark_escaped`, `services.auction.create_listing_by_token` for buddies), so the check rejected every escape spawn + every buddy AH listing. Migration `0189` re-adds both: `('owned', 'shelter', 'stored', 'escaped', 'auction')`. No data cleanup needed -- the migration only widens the constraint.
- **`,items` sort + kind dropdown stop silently failing.** `ItemsView._fetch` had a leftover `sort_clause` entry referring to `unit_usd_raw DESC NULLS LAST` -- a column my native-catalog-price refactor removed from the SELECT. Switching the sort to "usd" produced a SQL `column "unit_usd_raw" does not exist` error which discord.py logged as `Ignoring exception in view <ItemsView> for item <Button label='Sort'>` (and same for the kind select on the next interaction). The Python-side per-row pricing pass + `rows.sort(key=...)` already handled USD ordering correctly, so the fix is just to remove the dead SQL reference -- the visible sort behaviour is unchanged for the player.
- **Graceful shutdown is actually graceful now.** Railway redeploys produced a `Fatal startup error: ValueError: I/O operation on closed file.` line plus `RuntimeError: Event loop stopped before Future completed.` on every push, which Railway then categorised as a crash. Two fixes in `main.py`: (1) the SIGTERM handler no longer calls `loop.stop()` on the second signal -- that was killing `bot.close()` mid-flight; SIGKILL handles a hung shutdown ~10s later, and we shouldn't try to "force exit" ourselves. (2) New `_BOT_RUNNING` flag flips True after `bot.wait_until_ready()`. Exceptions caught while it's True log as `"Runtime error after startup"` instead of `"Fatal startup error"`; the specific `ValueError("I/O operation on closed file")` race during teardown logs as `"Shutdown teardown noise (safe to ignore)"` and exits 0. Clean redeploys no longer surface as crashes.

### More `_refresh` collisions + drs_commands diag downgrade
- **Renamed `_refresh` → `_redraw` in three more views.** `_StatusView` and `_PickerView` in `cogs/expeditions.py` plus `_EggPickerView` in `cogs/fishing.py` plus `_DelveRoomView` in `cogs/dungeon.py` were all shadowing `discord.ui.View`'s sync `_refresh(components)` framework method, producing `RuntimeWarning: coroutine '_<View>._refresh' was never awaited` on every interaction. All renamed; framework method untouched. Same root cause as the earlier `_HubView` fix.
- **`drs_commands` diagnostic no longer warns when the feature is just unused.** Player reported "⚠️ drs_commands feature: not enabled" persisted even after granting access "a dozen times" -- the feature is opt-in per guild, so a never-granted state shouldn't be a warning at all. Demoted from `r.warn` to `r.ok` with `"disabled (opt-in -- .admin beta grant drs_commands @user/@role to enable)"` copy. Real failures (DB error reading `beta_features`) still warn.

### Cross-cog buddy passives + rarity-extra lanes + attractor wiring
- **5 new buddy bonus lanes** layered on top of the existing `chat / work / trade`: `fishing` (catch weight), `farming` (harvest qty), `delve` (mine ore yield), `craft` (reserved), `battle` (wild + arena XP). `buddies_config.BONUS_LANES` is now an 8-tuple; `BONUS_LANE_LABELS` carries player-readable strings.
- **Rarity-extra signature lanes.** New `RARITY_EXTRA_SIGNATURE_LANES = {1:0, 2:0, 3:1, 4:2, 5:3}` map: a Common buddy's species lane is its only signature; Rare gets +1 extra signature, Epic +2, Legendary +3 -- chosen deterministically by walking `BONUS_LANES` from the species' primary so two players' Legendary Zenny always buff the same four lanes. New helper `buddy_bonus_lanes_for(species, rarity_tier)` returns the full set.
- **`services/buddy_bonus.py` updated to use the helper.** Any lane in the buddy's `buddy_bonus_lanes_for` set gets the SIG ramp; everything else gets OFF. So a Legendary Zenny levels into +chat / +work / +trade / +fishing all at the fast ramp; a Common Zenny still only fast-ramps `chat`.
- **Cog services wired.** `fishing.cast_resolve` multiplies caught weight by `buddy_bonus(lane="fishing")`. `farming.harvest_plot` multiplies yield qty by `buddy_bonus(lane="farming")`. `dungeon.mine_ore` multiplies ore qty by `buddy_bonus(lane="delve")`. Wild-battle XP credits in `dungeon.resolve_wild_battle` / `fishing.resolve_wild_battle` and arena XP in `buddy_economy.resolve_arena_battle` multiply through `buddy_bonus(lane="battle")` so a battle-aligned Legendary stacks meaningfully on top of the floor / zone / tier scaling.
- **Buddy panel surfaces every active passive.** New `_passive_effects_field(species, level, rarity_tier)` block on the buddy panel embed shows `Species (Chat XP): +X.X%` plus a `Rarity (Work, Trade, Fishing): +X.X% each` row for Rare+ buddies. Numbers match what `services/buddy_bonus.py` actually grants so the panel never lies about the buff. Common buddies see only the species line; Rare / Epic / Legendary players see exactly which extra lanes their rarity unlocked.

### Battle Attractor properly wired across all three games
- **Attractor doubles wild-battle spawn chance in fishing / farming / delve.** Pre-fix the `,buddy attractor` purchase only affected the buddy panel display -- none of `services/fishing.py:cast_resolve`, `services/farming.py:roll_pending_wild_buddy`, or `services/dungeon.py:advance_room` consulted `attractor_active` before rolling the spawn. Each path now probes the attractor flag and multiplies the per-cast / per-tick / per-room wild-battle chance by 2.0 (capped at 1.0) when active.
- **`attractor_pulled` indicator on every encounter prompt.** Fishing's `CastResult` gets a new `attractor_pulled: bool` field; farming stamps `attractor_pulled: True` onto `pending_wild_buddy` JSONB; delve stamps it onto the `wild_buddy` payload. The fishing wild-encounter embed appends ``🧲 Battle Attractor pulled this encounter (your active boost lured a fight that wouldn't have spawned).``; the farming win/loss embed adds a `🧲 Battle Attractor` field; the delve wild-buddy room embed adds the same. Players can finally see their attractor doing work.

### Arena wins credit active-buddy XP
- **Same fix as wild battles, applied to the arena.** `services/buddy_economy.py:resolve_arena_battle` now credits the active buddy via the canonical `services.buddy_battle.award_battle_xp` helper on every win. New constants `ARENA_XP_REWARD_BASE = 30 / per_level = 2.0 / max = 250` and a `arena_xp_reward(level)` helper define the curve. The clean-fight `bonus_pct` and the player's tier `bud_mult` stack the same way they do for BUD and BBT, so a Diamond-tier player on a clean Lv 30 fight pays roughly `(30 + 29*2.0) * 1.30 * 2.0 ≈ 230 XP` to their fighter. `ArenaResolution` gets `buddy_xp_awarded` + `fighter_buddy_id` for the cog-side receipt.

### Wild battles credit active-buddy XP
- **Delve + fishing wild-battle wins now grant XP to the active buddy.** Pre-fix the buddy that actually fought walked away with nothing on its row -- only the player got RUNE / ore / BBT (delve) or LURE / REEL / BBT (fishing). Both `services/dungeon.py:resolve_wild_battle` and `services/fishing.py:resolve_wild_battle` now look up the player's active buddy on a win and call the canonical `services.buddy_battle.award_battle_xp` helper to credit XP, mirroring how PvP and the chat-XP path persist progression.
- **Two new config helpers** (`dungeon_config.wild_battle_xp_reward(floor, rarity_tier)` and `fishing_config.wild_battle_xp_reward(zone_tier, rarity_tier)`) compute the XP per win. Delve scales `25 + 8*floor` with a `+10%` per opponent rarity tier (Floor 1 Common ~33 XP, Floor 10 Legendary ~140 XP). Fishing uses the same `WILD_BATTLE_*_PER_ZONE_TIER` curve as the LURE/REEL prizes (Zone 1 Common 25 XP, Zone 5 Legendary ~75 XP). The clean-fight `bonus_pct` multiplier applies on top so a perfect-round win pays a real XP bonus.
- **`WildBattleResolution`** dataclass on both services gets two new fields: `buddy_xp_awarded` (the int credited) and `fighter_buddy_id` (the cc_buddies.id that received it). Receipt-side rendering of the XP can layer on top in a follow-up; the data is in the result so the cog can pick it up immediately.
- The XP credit is wrapped in its own try/except so a failure (e.g. the buddy was sold mid-battle) doesn't roll back the RUNE / ore / LURE / REEL the player already saw.

### Bug fixes from prod logs
- **chat_level_up no longer FK-errors when an unregistered user gains chat XP.** Players who only chat (never run a registered command) don't have a `users` row yet, so the achievement `grant()` path tripped `fk_user_badges_user` on every chat-level milestone. `services/achievements.py:grant` now calls `db.ensure_user(uid, gid)` (idempotent INSERT ... ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING) before the `user_badges` INSERT, seeding the parent row if the user is brand new.
- **`,today` no longer logs `coroutine '_HubView._refresh' was never awaited`.** `discord.ui.View` has a private sync `_refresh(components)` method that the framework calls when re-hydrating components. My async `_refresh` was shadowing it. Renamed to `_redraw` so the framework's method is untouched and the warning goes away.
- **`,buddy nest deposit` error now surfaces the real failure instead of "Please try again".** `services/buddy_breeding.py:deposit` was catching every exception and returning a generic `"Daycare deposit failed. Please try again."` -- which (a) said "Daycare" not "Nest" after the rename, and (b) hid the actual `IntegrityError` / `ValueError` / type-mismatch from the player. The catch now formats the exception class + message into the user-facing reply so player reports include the root cause; the log line stamps the same details. Also corrected leftover `daycare collect failed` / `daycare cancel failed` log lines to `nest`.
- **Buddy dropdown errors now surface to the user.** `_BuddySelect.callback` wraps the `_re_render` call in try/except. A failure in `_load_pages` / `_build_panel_embed` / `edit_message` used to leave Discord with no response within 3s and the user with the generic "this interaction failed" -- now an ephemeral `Couldn't rebuild buddy panel: <ExceptionClass>: <message>` lands so we can diagnose. Note: `View interaction referencing unknown view` warnings after a bot restart are a separate issue (non-persistent views don't survive restart); re-running `,buddy` after a deploy gives a fresh interactive panel.

### `,today` ready-feed accuracy pass
- **Trap probe now actually checks soak time.** Player feedback: "today is saying 'ready right now' for my traps when they're not ready, and telling me to collect them with `,fish trap` which is incorrect." Fixed both: the probe pulls `placed_crab_traps` JSONB, walks each trap, looks up `fishing_config.crab_trap_meta(key).soak_seconds`, and only counts entries where `placed_at + soak_seconds <= NOW()`. Hint now points at `,fish trap collect` (the actual collect command, not the parent group).
- **AH listings moved out of the "Ready right now" feed.** Active listings aren't a "ready to claim" signal -- a sold listing auto-credits the seller's wallet at settle time, no claim step exists. The count moved to the Activity rollup as `**N AH listings -- ,ah mine`, where it belongs alongside quest / challenge counters. The Activity field now also shows a friendly placeholder (`(quiet day -- send an expedition or fish?)`) instead of a stale "Longest streak / Total claims" line that had no real data after the streak unification.
- **Added `,work` ready hint.** New probe reads `users.last_work` against `Config.WORK_COOLDOWN`; trips a `💼 Your ,work shift is ready.` hint when the cooldown has elapsed. Sits next to the `,daily` hint so the morning routine surfaces both check-ins.
- **Added empty-plot prompt for the farm.** `🌱 N empty plots -- ,farm to plant.` fires when the player has plots that are `state='empty'` (sourced via the same `jsonb_array_elements` pattern as the ripe-plot probe, so one call gives both signals).
- **Skipped `,ape` / `,beg` ready hints.** Both commands use `core/framework/cooldowns.user_cooldown` which is `discord.ext.commands.cooldown` -- in-memory rate-limiter, no DB column to probe. Adding them would require wiring a Redis-side cooldown reader; out of scope for this iteration.
- **Skipped stones-ready-to-level-up.** Each stone type (hashstones, lockstones, vaultstones, liqstones, gambastones + themed) has its own table with per-stone XP curves; computing "is this stone over its next-level XP threshold AND can the player afford the levelup cost?" needs a service helper that doesn't exist yet. Will add when the auto-levelup notification path gets refactored.

### Buddy crafted-food rebalance + cooldown
- **Crafted XP food rebalanced.** `services/crafting.py:_apply_buddy_effect` -- `buddy/xp` (Training Brew) was +500 XP, now +100. `buddy/xp_big` (Harvest Pie) was +1500 XP, now +300. The two were outpacing every other XP source by an order of magnitude; the new values plus the cooldown below put crafted food on par with passive chat / battle / expedition gain.
- **30-minute shared cooldown on crafted food.** Migration `0188_buddy_craft_cooldown.sql` adds `cc_buddies.last_buddy_craft_apply_at TIMESTAMPTZ`. Every `feed / play / restore / xp / xp_big / feast / full_revive` apply now stamps it; the next apply within 1800s is rejected with a friendly `wait Xm Ys` error. DB-side `EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (NOW() - col))` so container drift can't bypass it. `reroll_rarity` and the permanent-buff effects skip the gate -- those are limited by their own `max_stack: 1` already.

### `,today` Claim Daily delegates to `,daily` (unified cooldown + reward)
- **One daily, two surfaces.** Player feedback: "the daily bonus on the today command is tied to a different daily than the daily command?" -- yes, it was. The hub's Claim Daily button used to credit a separate hub-only reward off `user_daily_streak`, while `,daily` (earn cog) credited a wealth-scaled / job-perk-layered / buddy-bonus-multiplied reward off `users.last_daily`. Two cooldowns, two rewards, one confused player.
- Hub's button now delegates to `Earn._do_daily(ctx)` via `interaction.client.get_cog("Earn")`. Single 24h cooldown gate (`users.last_daily`), single reward stream (the full earn flow), single streak counter (`users.daily_streak`). Falls back to the legacy hub claim path if the Earn cog is unavailable, so the button still does something in test envs.
- `services/hub.streak_status` now reads `users.daily_streak` + `users.last_daily` directly, so the hub panel's `🔥 N-day streak` header and "claimed today?" indicator always match what `,daily` reports.

### AH buddy + egg listings now show rarity by NAME
- **Active buddy listings get backfilled with live `cc_buddies` data.** Migration `0187_buddy_listing_meta_backfill.sql` walks every active buddy listing and merges the live row's `level / rarity_tier / name / species / xp / gender / wins / losses / buddy_id` into `auction_listings.metadata`. Pre-existing listings created before the `create_listing_by_token` refresh fix landed had only the token's mint-time metadata (often missing `rarity_tier`), so the AH browse + inspect render fell through to a "Tier 1" default on every buddy regardless of actual rarity.
- **Render rarity by NAME everywhere.** Browse rows, the inspect embed, and the `,ah inspect <token>` token-detail embed now render rarity as `**Legendary** (T5)` / `**Rare** (T3)` / `**Common** (T1)` instead of the raw `Tier N`. Fall back gracefully to the T-prefix when `buddies_config` is unavailable. Eggs get the same treatment (`**Rare** Wecco` instead of `Tier 3 Wecco`). Listings whose metadata is genuinely missing `rarity_tier` now skip the field entirely instead of silently displaying "Tier 1" on every buddy.

### `,shop buy <stone>` no longer requires the currency arg
- **`,shop buy bloomstone` just works.** The cog signature defaulted `currency="DSD"`, which `_buy_stone` then rejected against the stone's `accepted_currencies` tuple -- so Bloomstone (HRV-only), Hashstone (BTC), Tidestone (REEL), Bloodstone (BBT), etc. all forced the player to remember and type the right token. Default is now an empty string; the existing `currency = (currency or "").upper().strip() or accepted[0]` fallback inside `_buy_stone` picks the stone's first accepted currency. Consumables (validator_guard / yield_guard / specialty_slot) still default to DSD via an explicit fallback in the consumable branch, so the legacy behaviour there is unchanged.

### "Daycare" -> "Nest" rename + Shop Quick Buy wired
- **Buddy daycare is now "the nest" everywhere players see it.** `,buddy daycare` is renamed to `,buddy nest` (with `daycare` / `breed` / `breeding` / `incubator` kept as aliases for muscle-memory). Embed titles drop "Daycare" for "Nest", the panel emoji moves from baby-bottle (👶) to nest (🪹), and every error / receipt / hint refers to "the nest" -- in `services/buddy_breeding.py`, `services/lexicon.py`, `services/hub.py`, `cogs/buddy.py`, `cogs/hub.py`, `quests_config.py`, and `achievements_config.py`. The DB table stays `cc_buddy_daycare` and the bus event stays `daycare_egg_collected` so historical data + active subscribers never break.
- **`,shop` Quick Buy actually buys now.** The Quick Buy button on the shop hub view used to pop a modal that just said "go retype `,shop buy <item>`" -- two extra steps for nothing. The modal now resolves the Shop cog via `interaction.client.get_cog("Shop")` and invokes `shop_buy(ctx, item, currency)` directly, so the player types the item, hits submit, and lands on the existing Confirm dialog inline. Failure paths fall back to the original "type the command" hint so the modal degrades gracefully if the cog ever loads under a different name.

### Bug fixes: extra buddy slots + AH buddy escrow + listing detail
- **Extra buddy slots are honored on every capture / hatch / adopt path.** `services/buddy_economy.user_max_buddies(db, gid, uid)` already returned the correct per-player cap (base + slots purchased via `,buddy slot buy`), but most pre-flight checks compared against the bare `MAX_OWNED_BUDDIES` constant (default 3). The result was players with extra slots being told their shelter is full at 3 owned buddies. Fixed at every callsite: `services/buddy_lifecycle.py` (adopt / reclaim / storage release), `services/buddy_world.py` (wild adopt), `services/buddy_market.py` (gift recipient cap), `services/dungeon.py` (delve capture), `services/farming.py` (farm capture), and `services/fishing.py` (egg lay + held-egg hatch). All routes now resolve the cap dynamically per-user.
- **Listing a buddy on the AH actually removes it from your collection.** The token-id list path (`,ah list <buddy_id> <price>` and the `List on AH` button) escrowed the NFT (`item_instances.owner_user_id = NULL`) but never touched `cc_buddies.status`, so the listed buddy stayed visible in `,buddy`, was still battleable, was still chosen by every "active buddy" lookup, and could be deployed on an expedition while sitting on the market. `services/auction.py:create_listing_by_token` now flips the matching `cc_buddies.status` to `'auction'` and clears `is_active` inside the same atomic block; the buddy_id is stamped into listing metadata so `cancel_listing` can flip it back to `'owned'` and `buy_listing` can transfer ownership to the buyer at sale time.
- **Buddy listings show fresh level / rarity / name.** Token metadata is a snapshot from mint time, so a buddy hatched at L1 and grown to L30 was still advertised on the AH as L1. `create_listing_by_token` now refreshes `level / rarity_tier / name / gender / hunger / happiness / energy / wins / losses` from the live `cc_buddies` row at list time, so the "Lv.30 T4 Sparky" badge in `,ah browse` matches what the seller actually surrendered.
- **`,ah browse` listing picker is more discoverable.** The row-2 dropdown that opens the full inspect view (Buy / Cancel / Refresh) was placeholder-labelled `"Open a listing for Buy / Cancel..."`. Renamed to `"Pick a listing to inspect / buy..."` so players actually find it. The picker has always done the "view more about the item" job; the label was hiding it.
- **Shop insufficient-balance error spells out the conversion math.** `,shop buy <stone> <currency>` now appends the network key the bot looked up, plus a one-line `Oracle: 1 HRV = $X -- need ~Y HRV to cover the $Z target` when the player's wallet probe came up short. Diagnoses bloomstone-can't-buy-with-HRV reports without needing the player to dig for oracle prices.

### `,today` ready-feed expansion + quick-collect buttons
- **More "ready right now" probes.** `,today` now also surfaces ripe farm plots, placed crab traps, a low-stat active buddy, and the `,daily` earn check-in alongside the existing eggs / daycare / expeditions / AH hints. The farm probe is rewritten to count rows where `(p->>'ready_at')::timestamptz <= NOW()` via `jsonb_array_elements` so it counts only plots actually ready to harvest, not "anything planted." The `,daily` probe reads `users.last_daily` directly (the column the earn cog stamps) so the hint never disagrees with the command-side gate. Hungry buddy hint trips when active buddy hunger / happiness / energy is below 30 -- pet, feed, or talk.
- **Row-2 quick-collect buttons.** Three new action buttons on the panel that each light up only when their target has something to claim:
  - **Collect Runs** -- sweeps every ready expedition through `services.expeditions.collect_expedition`; reports an aggregate count via ephemeral receipt.
  - **Hatch Egg** -- pops the oldest held egg through `services.fishing.hatch_held_egg` and announces what hatched.
  - **Daycare** -- mirrors `,buddy daycare collect`: graduates the egg via `services.buddy_breeding.collect`, slots it through `give_held_egg`, fires `daycare_egg_collected` on the bus so achievements / quests still tick.
- **Auto-disable on dead targets.** `_HubView._sync_button_states` reads the new `HubSummary.eggs_held / daycare_ready / expeditions_ready` counts and disables each quick-collect button when its target is empty. Saves the player a click on a button that would just say "nothing to do."

### Expeditions wired into hub / quests / achievements
- **`,today` panel surfaces ready expeditions.** `services/hub.py:_ready_to_claim_hints` now includes a single CTE-style probe over `buddy_expeditions` that counts `ready` (ends_at <= NOW()) and `running` (ends_at > NOW()) rows in one round-trip. The "Ready right now" feed shows `🎒 N expeditions ready -- ,expedition collect.` when any are collectable, or a softer `🎒 N expeditions still running -- ,expedition to check time left.` when there's only a pending run. The split mirrors what `,expedition` does so the two surfaces never disagree.
- **Bus events emitted on every send + collect.** `cogs/expeditions.py` now publishes `expedition_started` (payload: destination / duration_seconds / buddy_id / species / rarity_tier / expedition_id) and `expedition_collected` (payload: destination / species / loot dict / xp_gained / happiness_delta / expedition_id). Publishes are wrapped in best-effort try/except so a flaky bus never blocks the success path.
- **Five expedition quest templates** in `quests_config.py`:
  - **Daily** -- *Pack a Lunch* (send 1, $200), *Welcome Home* (collect 2, $350)
  - **Weekly** -- *Frequent Flyer* (collect 5, $2k), *Salt and Coral* (1 Reef collect, $750), *Whisper of Ruins* (1 Ruins collect, $1.2k)
  - The destination-specific quests use the new `expedition_collected_<dest>` fan-out trigger (the quest engine fans the generic event out into per-destination ticks so the catalog can ask "complete a Reef expedition" without a custom handler).
- **Seven expedition achievement badges** in `achievements_config.py` under the existing `buddy` category:
  - **First Steps** (1 collect, $100), **Trail Blazer** (10, $500), **Career Adventurer** (50, $3k)
  - **Forest Friend / Reefwalker / Cave Crawler / Ruin Reader** -- one badge per destination on first collect, escalating reward by tier ($150 / $200 / $300 / $500). Catalog drives the achievement engine via `sync_catalog`, so they appear on next bot boot without any code-side migration.
- **Engine subscribers wired** in `services/quests.py` and `services/achievements.py`. The quest handler additionally fans the generic `expedition_collected` event out into a per-destination call (`progress_trigger(... "expedition_collected_reef")`) so destination quests fire without the cog publishing four separate events.

### `,expedition` -- AI Buddy Expeditions
- **Send your active buddy on an autonomous timed run.** New cog `cogs/expeditions.py` (alias `,exped` / `,trek` / `,exp`) opens a status panel with a picker view: pick one of four **destinations** (`Whispering Forest`, `Coral Reef`, `Forgotten Mine`, `Ancient Ruins`), pick a duration (`1h`, `4h`, `8h`, `12h`), tap **Send**. The buddy stays in your collection -- the expedition just snapshots their species / rarity / level at deploy time so changing your active buddy mid-run doesn't shift the rewards. When the timer expires the player runs `,expedition collect [id]` (or **Collect All** from the panel) and gets back a procedural story log + a weighted loot drop pulled from fishing / farming / delve pools. Each loot draw is independent so longer runs draw more times rather than draw better.
- **Per-destination loot pools and species affinity.** Each destination biases its loot toward a different bucket -- forests favor crops, reefs favor fish, mines favor ore, ruins favor RUNE. `expeditions_config.SPECIES_AFFINITY` maps every catalog species to its preferred destination (sea-types align with Reef, rock / construct types align with Mine, etc.). An affinity-matched run gets **+25% loot quantity** and a per-draw rarity bump; mismatched / neutral runs draw at base rates. Higher buddy rarity tiers also stack a flat per-draw multiplier (T1 = 1.0x, T5 = 1.4x).
- **Migration `0186_buddy_expeditions.sql`** adds the `buddy_expeditions` table (`expedition_id` PK, FK to `cc_buddies(id)` ON DELETE CASCADE, `destination`, `duration_seconds`, `started_at`, `ends_at`, `collected_at`, `story_json`, `loot_json`, `xp_gained`, `happiness_delta`, `status`, plus `species_at_start` / `rarity_at_start` / `level_at_start` for the deploy-time snapshot). A partial unique index on `buddy_id WHERE status = 'running'` enforces "one running expedition per buddy" at the schema level so two simultaneous Send taps can't double-deploy.
- **All time comparisons are server-side.** `list_active` selects `EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (ends_at - NOW()))` straight onto each row so the cog splits running vs. ready without ever calling `datetime.utcnow()`. The collect path locks the row with `FOR UPDATE`, reads the same DB-computed `seconds_remaining`, and refuses if it's still positive -- no container-vs-DB clock skew possible. Ore + RUNE wallet credits and per-draw NFT mints all happen inside the same `db.atomic()` block as the `status='collected'` stamp so a partial failure leaves the row in `running` for the player to retry.
- **Procedural story generator** lives in `services/expeditions.py:_generate_story`. Composes a 5-paragraph run log: a destination opener + 3 random destination events (sampled without replacement) + a closer, with `{name}` / `{species}` / `{dest}` / `{item}` substitution. The `{item}` token pulls a real-loot word from the run when possible (`a chunk of copper`, `eggplant`, `Rusted Tin Can`) and falls back to a flavor placeholder when the run dropped nothing. 32 events across the four destinations as a starter pool; trivial to extend by adding strings to `expeditions_config.EVENTS`.

### Button-based egg + buddy selection
- **`,fish egg` is now an interactive picker.** The status embed stays the same, but a new owner-locked view rides along: a row-0 dropdown lists every (species, rarity) bucket the player holds (`Common Wecco Egg ×4`, `Rare Zenny Egg ×1`, ...), and four action buttons on row 1 act on the current selection -- **Hatch** (immediate, oldest matching), **Sell** (modal: qty / `all`), **Gift** (modal: recipient + qty), **List on AH** (modal: price / currency, routes through `services.auction.create_listing(kind="egg", ref="<species>:<tier>")` so the existing `_lock_egg` rarity-aware lock fires). Refresh re-fetches the held-eggs JSONB so a hatch in another channel updates the dropdown without re-running `,fish egg`. The legacy `,fish egg hatch / sell / gift` text subcommands keep working for muscle-memory.
- **`,buddy` panel adds a jump-to-buddy dropdown.** The live panel always paged across owned buddies via Prev/Next; row-3 now carries a `_BuddySelect` listing every owned buddy with rarity name + level + active marker (`Sparky -- L12 Rare (active)`). Click an option to jump straight to that buddy's page -- no Prev/Next clickfest through a 20-buddy collection. The dropdown rebuilds on every re-render (initial paint, button click, and the passive live tick) so newly hatched / sold / gifted buddies appear immediately. Discord's 25-option select cap is respected; past 25 buddies the select disables and Prev/Next remains the fallback.

### `,today` -- daily front-door panel + login streak
- **One command, every relevant signal in one place.** `,today` (aliases `,routine` / `,login`) opens an owner-locked interactive panel with the player's daily-routine info: streak status (`🔥🔥 14-day streak`), today's claim button, net-worth headline, the top 3 active quests with progress bars, a "ready right now" feed (eggs ready to hatch, daycare ready to collect, plots growing, active AH listings), a Refresh button, and four cog-jump buttons (Fish / Farm / Delve / AH / Items) that pop ephemeral pointers to the right command. Drop-in entry point for new players who don't know what to do next, and a fast morning routine for veterans. (Originally shipped as `,hub` / `,daily` / `,home`; renamed after a deploy collision -- `,hub` was already an alias on `,menu` (minigames) and `,daily` was `cogs/earn.py`'s 24h check-in.)
- **Daily login streak with USD-pegged rewards.** Migration `0185_user_daily_streak.sql` adds `user_daily_streak` (one row per user/guild) tracking `current_streak`, `longest_streak`, `last_claim_utc`, `total_claims`, `total_reward_usd_raw`. The Claim button in `,today` runs once per UTC day inside a single `db.atomic()` transaction (so rapid double-clicks can't double-credit) and pays `0.50 * min(streak, 30)` USD into the wallet, with milestone bonuses on day 7 (`+$3`), day 14 (`+$7`), and day 30 (`+$25`). The base reward saturates at the 30-day cap so perpetual logins keep paying without runaway inflation; missing a day resets the streak to 1 on the next claim.
- **`services/hub.py:hub_summary` is the single aggregator** -- one call returns net worth via the canonical `compute_net_worth`, top quests via `services.quests.current_for_user`, active challenge count via `services.challenges.list_active`, and per-cog "ready" hints from light targeted queries. Each subsystem is wrapped in try/except so a busted helper degrades the matching panel row instead of 500-ing the whole hub.

### Per-item lexicon detail
- **`,db <name>` now answers "where do I get this?" specifically.** `services/lexicon.py` was a thin per-kind copy that said the same thing for every fish, every weapon, every recipe. It now loads the actual catalog dict and surfaces real per-item detail: fish list their **zones, rod-tier requirement, lbs range, LURE/lb sell rate**, and which crafting recipes they feed into; bait shows **REEL price + fish/rare/bonus pull bonuses**; crops show **rarity, season, growth time, yield range, HRV/unit sell price, downstream recipes**; weapons / armor show **tier badge + ATK/DEF + RUNE price + equip command**; consumables show **effect copy derived from `kind`/`value`** (heal %, mine_boost %, charm %, lure %, revive %, escape, damage scrolls); crafted recipes list **inputs, FGD fee, specialty + locked flag, min level, apply target**; ore points at the AMM + stake commands and notes the fungible token shape; stones / shop items pull the catalog blurb and link the relevant `,shop` subcommands. Catalog imports are cached so repeated `,db` calls don't re-import the modules.

### `,items` and `,db` row layout cleanup
- **Two-line rows so embeds stop overflowing.** The single-line `🪱 **Earth Worm** · `bait.worm` · x500 · `1 REEL` · `$0.05` ea · `$25.00` total -- example `lur:af09c12`` was 130+ chars and wrapped messily inside Discord's 50-char field column. Each owned-contract entry in `,items` overview / `,items list` and each catalog entry in `,db browse` is now rendered as a head line (`{emoji} **Name** ×count · T1`) plus a muted (`-#`) sub line (`` `address` · `1.00 REEL` · `$0.05` ``). The "example sample id" cruft is dropped since the address is the actionable handle. Per-chunk cap drops from 25 to 15 entries to stay under the 1024-char field limit with the two-line format.

### Catalog prices in `,items` and `,db`
- **Native catalog prices on every contract.** Most catalogs quote in their network token, not USD: bait in REEL, weapons / armor / consumables in RUNE, crafted in FGD, crops in HRV. The bootstrap was only filling `item_contracts.base_price_raw` (USD), and even that read the wrong field names (`price_usd` / `sell_usd`, neither of which exists), so almost every kind rendered with no price at all. Migration `0184_item_contract_native_price.sql` adds `base_price_native_raw` + `base_price_currency` columns; `services/nft_bootstrap.py` now reads `price_reel` (BAIT) / `price_rune` (WEAPONS, ARMOR, CONSUMABLES) / `fgd_cost` (CRAFT_ITEMS) / `hrv_sell_price` (CROPS) into the native pair, and `cost_stable` (SHOP_ITEMS) keeps landing in the USD column. Crafted / crop / fish rarity tiers also get back-derived from the catalog `rarity` string (common -> 1, ..., legendary -> 5) since none of those catalogs use `rarity_tier` directly.
- **Single price renderer** (`services/item_pricing.render_catalog_price`) used by `,items` overview / `,items list` / `,items inspect` / `,items contract` and `,db browse` / `,db <name>`. Format mirrors the AH: ``120.00 RUNE  ·  $45.21`` when both sides exist, native-only or USD-only when one is missing. The USD half is oracle-converted at display time when only the native price is recorded, so a dry catalog still shows a USD estimate.
- **Sort by USD** in `,items` now uses the unified per-row USD value (last sale, then catalog USD, then oracle-converted native) instead of the partial `COALESCE(last_sold, base_price_raw)` the SQL did before. Worm bait + iron sword + crops finally land next to each other when sorted by value.

### Bug Fixes
- **`,craft apply harvest_pie` no longer errors with `Unknown buddy effect: xp_big`**: `crafting_config.py` defines `harvest_pie` with a "+1500 XP for the active buddy" effect (`apply: buddy/xp_big`), but `services/crafting.py:_apply_to_buddy` only handled `xp` (+500). Players who crafted a Harvest Pie hit a hard `ValueError` on apply, losing the craft. Added the missing `xp_big` branch -- a successful apply now grants the active buddy +1500 XP as advertised.
- **`,delve mine` now honours every `mine_boost` consumable, not just pickaxe oil**: The mine action hardcoded `pickaxe_oil` (+50%) so Diamond Pickaxe Oil (`diamond_pickaxe`, value 1.50, "Cracks the rock open. +150% ore") was banked but never consumed. `services/dungeon.py:mine_ore` now walks the player's consumables, asks `dungeon_config.consumable_meta` for any `kind == "mine_boost"`, picks the highest-value one, applies its multiplier (`qty *= 1.0 + value`) and burns one. `,delve use diamond_pickaxe` followed by `,delve mine` now yields 2.5x ore, and future `mine_boost` consumables plug in automatically.

### Mid-room consumables, Plant All, in-cast bait swap
- **`,delve` mid-room consumables select** -- new row-2 dropdown on the room panel lists every consumable you own (heals / buffs / scrolls) with quantities. Selecting one runs `dsvc.use_consumable` immediately, re-renders the room embed (HP refreshed, qty decremented, dropdown rebuilt), and surfaces the receipt as an ephemeral so the main panel stays clean. Auto-disabled with explanatory placeholder when you have no consumables. Doesn't fire inside combat -- escape-class items still need to be used from the battle view.
- **`,farm` Plant All button** (row 1, 🌱 success) -- plants your "best" seed packets into every empty plot in one tap. Best = highest-rarity first (legendary -> common, then alphabetical), walking packets in order until either every empty plot is filled or you run out of seeds. Single transaction per plot via `farm_svc.plant_seed` so a partial run still records the plots that succeeded. Posts an ephemeral receipt grouped by crop ("🌽 Corn x2, 🥔 Potato x1"). Refreshes the field embed + the seed/plot dropdowns immediately.
- **`,fish` cast-result bait dropdown** -- the post-cast `_CastResultView` now ships with a row-1 bait equip dropdown so you can swap bait between casts without opening `,fish stats`. New `_CastResultBaitSelect.build()` async-hydrates options from your live inventory at attach time. On pick: runs `fish_svc.set_bait`, sends ephemeral `🪱 Equipped Worm.`, the next Cast Again uses the new bait.

## [main] -- 2026-04-30

### New Features
- **Farming field buttons**: The `,farm` embed now has interactive buttons -- **Harvest All** (green), **Water All** (blue), **Sell All** (grey), and **Refresh** (grey) -- plus a Bump button. Each action runs in-place and updates the embed so players never have to type a follow-up command for the most common field operations.

### Bug Fixes
- **Fishing hook timer accuracy**: The bite-window reaction timer (`_bite_at`) was stamped before the Discord HTTP edit round-trip, so Discord latency (200ms-3s) was counted against the player's 3-second window. The stamp now happens after the edit ACK, ensuring `reaction_seconds` measures true player reaction time and the sweet-hook bonus / late penalty apply correctly.
- **`,ah` crash -- `'str' object has no attribute 'get'`**: Auction-house listing rows store `metadata` as a JSON string in the DB. Six call-sites in `cogs/auction.py` used `(row.get("metadata") or {})` to parse it, which returns the raw string when metadata is non-empty (strings are truthy, so the `or {}` fallback never fired). All six sites now use `auc._as_dict()` which handles string-encoded JSON correctly.
- **`,ah buy` settlement: better diagnostics + buddy-by-name fix**: The catch-all in `cogs/auction.py` now surfaces the actual exception class + message ("Could not settle listing #N: `IntegrityError: ...`") instead of the unhelpful "try again" so players hitting a constraint or asyncpg error can report what went wrong without log access. Also fixed `_deliver_buddy` / `_return_buddy` in `services/auction.py` which used `int(ref)` to derive the buddy id -- that crashed with a ValueError on every name-listed buddy ("Sparky"), since `ref` is the seller-typed string. Both helpers now resolve through `metadata.buddy_id` (which `_lock_buddy` stamps on at list time), with `int(ref)` only as a fallback for legacy rows. `_deliver_egg` now raises a clear ValueError if the buyer's `user_fishing` row can't be initialised, replacing the prior silent-zero-row UPDATE that debited the buyer without delivering the egg.

### Changes
- **Eggs are genderless until they hatch**: Migration 0174 pre-rolled a gender on every held egg + daycare egg so the player saw the eventual buddy gender ahead of time. That conflicts with the design intent: eggs are eggs, gender is rolled at the moment they hatch into a buddy. Migration `0175` reverses it -- drops `cc_buddy_daycare.egg_gender`, strips the `gender` key from every entry in `user_fishing.held_eggs`, and from `auction_listings.metadata` / `item_instances.metadata` for `kind='egg'`. `cc_buddies.gender` is unchanged (buddies still have a real, canonical gender once hatched, and breeding still requires one ♂ + one ♀ parent). Code-side: `services/fishing.py` no longer rolls gender at lay time, the held-egg JSONB shape no longer carries `gender`, and every hatch path (`fish_for_egg` direct hatch, `hatch_held_egg`, daycare collect via `give_held_egg`) rolls gender fresh at the cc_buddies INSERT. Display: `,fish egg`, `,ah browse`, `,ah inspect`, and `,ah token` no longer show a glyph next to eggs. The `,ah list egg <species>:<gender>` filter is removed (eggs have no gender to filter by); `,ah list egg <species>:<tier>` still works.

### Gap fixes
- **AH cancel + buy now respect token-path listings**. The new `create_listing_by_token` flow doesn't touch JSONB inventory on creation, but `cancel_listing` was still calling `_RETURN_HANDLERS` (re-adding inventory the seller never lost) and `buy_listing` was still calling `_DELIVER_HANDLERS` (giving the buyer JSONB inventory on top of the NFT they were already getting). Both paths accumulated drift on every cycle. Fix: `services/auction.py:create_listing_by_token` now stamps `metadata.path = "token"` on the listing row; `cancel_listing` / `buy_listing` check that flag and skip the legacy JSONB handler when set. Token-path listings only ever change state via the NFT escrow / sweep, which is what we wanted.
- **`,db <name>` detail footer now suggests `,ah list <key> <price>`** when you actually own the item. Lets players go from "look up worm bait" -> "list my worm bait" without leaving the embed.

### `,group lp` -- founder treasury <-> LP
- **Founder-only treasury / LP plumbing** for the group's `<group_token>/USD` AMM pool. The founder can push a bounded percentage of the vault into the pool's group-token reserve, or pull a bounded percentage of the pool's reserve back into the vault. Single-sided ops -- only the group-token side of the pool moves, so price will shift, and the founder accepts that.
- **Safeguards** all enforced in `services/group_lp.py`:
  - **Founder-only** -- caller's user_id must match `mining_groups.founder_id`. Guild admins are not auto-authorised.
  - **Master kill switch** -- `treasury_lp_unlocked` must be TRUE. The founder flips it via `,group lp enable` / `,group lp disable`.
  - **Per-action pct cap** -- 25%. A larger pct raises a clear error.
  - **24h cooldown** between actions, checked off the DB clock (`EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (NOW() - last_treasury_lp_at))`).
  - **Bounded price impact** -- a deposit can't move more than 25% of the current pool reserve in one shot, so a single op can't shock-move price by more than the same fraction.
  - **Confirm dialog** before either action runs.
  - **Audit trail** -- every successful op writes a `GROUP_LP_DEPOSIT` / `GROUP_LP_WITHDRAW` row to `tx_log`.
- **Commands** (in `cogs/groups.py`):
  - `,group lp` -- usage / help.
  - `,group lp status` -- treasury balance, pool reserves, lifetime deposited, lock state, last-action timestamp.
  - `,group lp enable` / `,group lp disable` -- master switch.
  - `,group lp deposit <pct>` -- push pct% of vault into LP.
  - `,group lp withdraw <pct>` -- pull pct% of pool reserve out.
- **Migration `0183`** adds three columns to `mining_groups`: `treasury_lp_unlocked` (BOOLEAN, default FALSE), `last_treasury_lp_at` (TIMESTAMPTZ), `treasury_lp_total_raw` (NUMERIC(36,0), lifetime deposited).

### `,shop` quick buy + buddy panel List on AH
- **`,shop` hub** picks up two new row-1 buttons:
  - 🛒 **Quick Buy** -- opens a Discord modal asking for the item key + optional currency. Submission posts an ephemeral hint with the exact `,shop buy <key> [currency]` to confirm. Doesn't bypass the per-item ConfirmView (each shop path keeps its own confirmation loop), but the modal saves the player from typing the key into chat.
  - 🔄 **Refresh** -- re-renders the current section (handy after a stone level-up or guard buy elsewhere).
- **`,buddy` panel** adds a row-1 🏛 **List on AH** button next to Rename + Refresh. Click pops a price modal pre-bound to the panel's current-page buddy; submission resolves the buddy's NFT via `find_owned_buddy_token` and runs `create_listing_by_token` so the gas / NFT escrow / event log all stay consistent. Refuses cleanly when the buddy has no NFT, the wrong owner, or is already escrowed.

### `,me` is the navigation hub
- **`,me` showcase** gets two rows of quick-jump buttons (rows 2 + 3) that link to every interactive panel:
  - 📦 **Items** -> `,items` (NFT browser)
  - 🏛 **AH** -> `,ah` (auction house)
  - 📖 **Lexicon** -> `,db` (item lookup + sources)
  - 🔨 **Craft** -> `,craft list`
  - 🎣 **Fish** -> `,fish stats`
  - 🌾 **Farm** -> `,farm`
- Each click sends an ephemeral hint with the exact command + a one-line blurb so the player can copy / re-run without leaving the showcase. Owner-locked. Tab picker (row 0) and Bump (row 1) unchanged. The showcase becomes the discoverability hub for everything else.

### Prices everywhere: `,db browse` + `,ah browse` get USD columns
- **`,db browse`** rows now show price inline. Priority: most-recent **sale** (network coin + USD snapshot at sale time) -> falls back to the **catalog base price** (USD only) when nothing has settled yet. CTE pulls each contract's last sold event in one round trip so the page render stays fast even at 200 rows.
- **`,ah browse`** rows now show a `~$X.XX` USD equivalent next to the listed-currency price. Live-oracle multiplied per page (cached per unique currency on the page so 8 LURE listings = 1 oracle lookup, not 8). Same render path is reused by `,ah search` results.
- New `_oracle_map_for_rows(db, gid, rows)` helper in `cogs/auction.py` -- builds the symbol -> oracle-price map for a page slice; passed into the existing `_browse_row_line` + `_build_browse_embed` via a new optional `oracle_map` param so legacy callers keep working unchanged.

### Plot targeting + cast-result panel button
- **`,farm` plot-target dropdown (row 3)**: pick exactly which plot the next seed plant lands in (default still "next empty"). Picking a plot also re-renders the seed dropdown's placeholder so it reads "Plant seed into Plot #N..." and the seed pick goes there. Resets to "next empty" automatically after each successful plant so chained plants flow naturally.
  - Plot rows show plot number + state + crop name + emoji so the player sees their field at a glance.
  - Disabled when the chosen plot isn't actually empty (e.g. you picked Plot #2 but Plot #2 is growing) -- placeholder explains why.
- **`,fish` cast result panel button**: the post-cast embed (`_CastResultView`) gets a 📋 **Panel** button next to Cast Again + Bump. Click pops the full `_FishStatsView` (bait dropdown + Cast button + Refresh) as a follow-up so the player can swap bait without leaving the cast loop.

### `,fish stats` + `,farm` get interactive dropdowns
- **`,fish stats` (self only)**: new `_FishStatsView` adds a row-0 **Equip bait** dropdown that lists every bait you own (with counts), plus a row-1 **Cast** button + Refresh. Selecting a bait calls `fish_svc.set_bait` and refreshes the panel; Cast hands off to the existing animated cast flow so the bite-window UX stays unchanged. Looking at someone else's stats stays a static embed (no actions make sense for them).
- **`,farm` field view** now has a **Plant** dropdown (row 2) listing every seed packet you own (with counts). Selecting a seed plants ONE into the **next empty plot** (`farm_svc.plant_seed`). Dropdown auto-disables when you have no packets OR no empty plots, with the placeholder text explaining why. Rebuilt on every Refresh / Harvest / Water / Sell so packet counts + empty-plot detection stay live.
- **`,inventory` footer** now mentions `,items` so players migrating to the NFT browser have a discovery path.

### `,craft list` is now an interactive recipe browser
- **Mining-panel style**: owner-locked 5-min timeout, dropdown to filter, dropdown to pick + craft, Prev / Next / Refresh buttons.
  - **Specialty dropdown** (row 0): All / Smithing / Alchemy / Cooking / Fletching / Tinkering. Page resets when you switch.
  - **Recipe-pick dropdown** (row 2): every recipe on the current page (up to 15) shown with emoji + name + rarity + specialty. Picking one calls `craft_item(qty=1)` immediately and posts the receipt as a follow-up so the browser stays open for the next pick.
  - **Prev / Next** (row 1): 15 recipes per page. Disabled at the boundaries.
  - **Refresh**: re-fetches your crafting level + recipe list (handy after a level-up).
- The old static panel (general/specialist/general split, wallet snapshot) is gone -- the new view is one clean recipes list with metadata on each line.
- Backed by a new `RecipesView` + `_RecipeSpecialtySelect` + `_RecipePickSelect` in `cogs/crafting.py`.

### Browse picker + Transfer modal
- **`,ah` browser** -- new row-2 dropdown lists every listing on the current page (kind emoji + label `#id  ·  ref` + price + kind sub-line). Selecting one opens the same `ListingActionView` (Buy / Cancel / Refresh) as `,ah inspect` would, as a follow-up message in the channel. Player can browse → buy without ever typing a listing id. Picker auto-rebuilds on Prev / Next / kind-change / sort.
- **`,items inspect`** -- new **Transfer** button on `TokenActionView`. Click pops a Discord modal with one field (`@user mention OR numeric user id`). Submission validates the recipient is a non-bot guild member, charges `transfer` gas in the network coin, runs `services.items.transfer`, and stamps the gas onto the most-recent transfer event so the inspect history shows it. Same hide-when-not-owner gate as the existing List button.

### Inspect views get action buttons
- **`,ah inspect <id>`** -- new `ListingActionView` adds three buttons (5-min owner-locked timeout):
  - **Buy** -- runs the same code path as `,ah buy <id>` for the invoking user. Hidden when you ARE the seller. Disabled / removed for non-active listings.
  - **Cancel** -- runs `,ah cancel <id>`. Visible only to the seller.
  - **Refresh** -- re-fetches the listing and re-renders the embed in place.
  - Embed-build code factored into `_build_listing_inspect_embed(row, prefix)` so Refresh doesn't duplicate the entire pipeline.
- **`,items inspect <token_id>`** -- new `TokenActionView`:
  - **List on AH** -- pops a Discord modal asking for price + optional currency, submits via `services.auction.create_listing_by_token`. Hidden when the caller doesn't own the token, or it's burned / escrowed.
  - **Refresh** -- ephemeral hint to re-run `,items inspect` (avoids re-rendering the entire history field on every click).
  - **View Contract** -- ephemeral hint pointing at `,items contract <address>`. Hidden when the token has no contract row.

### `,items` is now an interactive browser
- **`,items` opens an owner-locked, paginated, filterable view** (5-min timeout). Replaces the static "count by kind" overview.
  - **Kind dropdown** -- pick `All` or any of buddy / egg / fish / bait / junk / crop / weapon / armor / consumable / crafted / stone / shop. Page resets when you switch.
  - **Sort cycle button** -- count desc / USD desc / name asc.
  - **Prev / Next pagination** -- 8 contract rows per page.
  - **Refresh** -- re-fetches so freshly-minted (catch / craft / shop) and freshly-listed items show up immediately.
- **Per-row data**: emoji, name, contract address, count owned, per-unit USD (last sale or catalog), per-row total USD. Embed title carries the per-kind grand total.
- **Pattern matches the `,ah` browser** so the muscle memory transfers (`cogs/auction.py:BrowseView`).
- Subcommands `,items list / inspect / contracts / contract / transfer / help` are unchanged for power users.

### `,ah list <name> <price>` + NFT-only listing flow
- **`,ah list minnow 5`** is the new simplest form. Auto-resolves the bare name to the seller's oldest owned NFT of that contract (FIFO across `item_instances`), pulls category from contract metadata, and defaults currency to the network's home coin. No more typing `kind` or `ref` for the common case.
- **Fixes the "you only have 0 `minnow` (need 1)" bug**. Root cause: the token-id-driven path was still routing through the legacy `_lock_*` JSONB inventory handlers, so a JSONB row out of sync with the NFT layer would block listings even when the seller actually owned the NFT. `services/auction.py:create_listing_by_token` is now a standalone path that escrows the NFT directly (`owner_user_id = NULL` + `listing_id` pointer + `auction_listing_tokens` row) and writes the listing row + `list` event without touching JSONB. JSONB drift is what `,admin items reconcile` is for.
- **`services/auction.py:find_owned_token_for_contract(...)`** is the new resolver: takes a name / catalog_key / address, picks the matching contract (exact then fuzzy), and returns the seller's oldest owned token id of that contract. Used by the `,ah list <name> <price>` parse path.
- **Token displays drop the `#N` suffix**. `,items list` and `,items inspect` now show `bait:fd67e9ee` instead of `bait:fd67e9ee (#1)` -- the unit_index still lives on the row for ordering / debugging but isn't a player-facing surface.
- **`,ah help` rewritten** to lead with `<name> <price>`, then the token-id form, then the kind/ref power-user form. Default-currency-per-network table inline.

### Gas fees on every NFT state change
- **Every player-initiated NFT transaction now pays gas** in the network's native coin, the way real chains do. Schedule (flat per event):
  - `transfer` (`,items transfer`) -- **0.01 of the network coin**, paid by the sender.
  - `list` (`,ah list`) -- **0.05**, paid by the seller.
  - `unlist` (`,ah cancel`) -- **0.01**, paid by the seller.
  - `sold` (`,ah buy`) -- **0.10**, paid by the **buyer** on top of the listed price.
- **Network coin map** in `services/items.py`: `bud` -> BUD, `lur` -> LURE, `har` -> HRV, `cry` -> RUNE, `fge` -> INGOT, `dsc` -> DSC, `eth` -> ETH, `btc` -> BTC, `sun` -> SUN, `moon` -> MOON. Mints (catch / harvest / craft / shop / hatch) and burns (consumed in gameplay) don't pay gas -- those are gameplay outcomes, not signed transactions.
- **`services/items.py:charge_gas(...)`** is the canonical debit helper. Returns `(gas_raw, currency)` for the event-log stamp; raises `ValueError("Need ... for gas ...")` on insufficient balance so the caller can abort cleanly. Migration `0181` adds `gas_raw` + `gas_currency` columns to `item_token_events`.
- **Wired sites**:
  - `cogs/nft.py:nft_transfer` -- charges sender, stamps gas on the transfer event, footer notes the fee.
  - `services/auction.py:create_listing` -- charges seller before the listing INSERT (atomic rollback on debit failure); gas stamped on the primary token's `list` event.
  - `services/auction.py:cancel_listing` -- charges seller, stamps on primary `unlist` event.
  - `services/auction.py:buy_listing` -- charges buyer, stamps on primary `sold` event. Gas is on top of the price (real-NFT semantics).
- **`,items inspect` history field now shows the gas paid** for each event, e.g. `💰 12/25 14:30  ·  Sold  ·  @x -> @y  ·  5.00 LURE  ·  $12.34  ·  gas 0.1000 LURE`. Older events with `gas_raw IS NULL` (pre-migration-0181) just omit the gas tail.

### Per-token history + price displays
- **New `item_token_events` event log** (migration `0180`): one row per state transition on a token (`mint` / `transfer` / `list` / `unlist` / `sold` / `burn`), with from/to user ids, listing id, price (network coin + USD snapshot), and a metadata JSONB. Indexes for token-history walk, contract-history walk, and sold-only price aggregation.
- **`services/items.py` writes events on every state change**: `mint_unit` -> `mint`, `transfer` -> `transfer`, `burn_unit` -> `burn`. Best-effort try/except around each write so an event-log hiccup never breaks the underlying mint/transfer/burn.
- **`services/auction.py` writes `list` / `unlist` / `sold` events**: `create_listing` stamps a `list` event per escrowed token (with the listed price + currency); `cancel_listing` stamps `unlist`; `buy_listing` stamps `sold` per token with the per-unit slice of the listed price + a USD snapshot from the live oracle so historical reads don't drift.
- **`,items inspect` shows two new fields**:
  - **Last sale / Catalog price**: per-token price in the listed currency AND a USD snapshot (e.g. `5.00 LURE  ·  $12.34`). Falls back to the contract's `base_price_raw` (catalog price, already USD-scaled) when nothing has settled yet.
  - **History**: chronological list of up to the last 10 events with glyphs (🆕 mint, 🎁 transfer, 🏛 list, ↩ unlist, 💰 sold, 🔥 burn), timestamps, from/to mentions, and prices on sale events. Truncates safely under Discord's 1024-char field cap.
- **`,items` overview now shows a USD column per kind + a grand total in the title**. The overview's SQL aggregates each contract's last-sold-USD (or catalog `base_price_raw` when no sale has settled yet), summed across the user's owned units. Footer notes "USD = last sale or catalog price" so players know the pricing basis.
- **`,items list` rows show per-contract price** (network coin + USD if a sale has happened, otherwise USD-only catalog price), and the embed title carries a per-kind USD total.
- **New `services/item_pricing.py`** module: `usd_value_raw(currency, raw)` for oracle-driven USD conversion, `contract_price_summary(contract_id)` for last/avg/best/N sales, `estimate_token_value_usd(...)` for the per-token best-effort price used by the overview.

### `,ah list <token_id> <price>` -- token-id-driven listing
- **`,ah list bud:k889kak 50000`** (or `fge:fd67e9ee 100`, `lur:81819kak 25 LURE`, etc.) is the new preferred list form. The cog detects a `<network>:<hex>` token id as the first arg and routes to a new `services/auction.py:create_listing_by_token` helper that:
  1. Verifies the seller actually owns the token (not burned, not already escrowed in another listing, in this guild).
  2. Reads `kind` + `catalog_key` straight off the contract registry -- no manual category arg.
  3. Defaults currency to the kind's home network coin (`bud:...` -> BUD, `lur:...` -> LURE, `cry:...` -> RUNE, `fge:...` -> INGOT, `har:...` -> HRV) so `,ah list fge:fd67e9ee 100` lists for 100 INGOT without anyone typing it.
  4. Routes through the existing `create_listing` so the JSONB-side bookkeeping (cc_buddies status flip, held_eggs pop, count-map decrement) keeps working in this transition phase.
- **Legacy `,ah list <kind> <ref> [qty] <price>` form still works** unchanged. The parser tries the token-id form first (when arg 1 contains exactly one `:` and the tail is hex); otherwise falls through to the kind/ref dispatch.
- **`,ah help` updated** to document both forms with a copy-from-`,items inspect` hint.

### Item lexicon (`,db`) + premium third specialty slot
- **`,db` is a new player-facing item lexicon** (aliases: `,lexicon` / `,wiki` / `,find` / `,lookup`).
