Bare `,db` shows a count-by-kind overview. `,db browse [kind]` paginates every contract under a kind. `,db search <text>` fuzzy-matches across name / address / catalog_key. `,db <name>` or `,db <address>` jumps straight to a single item's detail card -- shows rarity, base price, full supply stats (alive / burned / total minted), how many you personally own, AND a "Where to get it" field with cog-specific acquisition steps (catch / craft / shop / mob drop / auction). Source copy lives in `services/lexicon.py` so adding a new kind or new acquisition path is a one-spot change. Backed by the `item_contracts` registry that the NFT bootstrap already populates -- adding a new item to a config dict gives it a lexicon entry on the next boot.
- **Premium third crafting-specialty slot** (`,shop buy specialty_slot`, $1,000,000 USD). Default `ACTIVE_SPECIALTY_CAP` is 2; one-time purchase bumps your effective cap to 3. Migration `0179` adds `user_crafting.extra_specialty_slots INTEGER DEFAULT 0` (with a CHECK to clamp 0..5 for future scaling). Buy flow charges in USD off the wallet, refuses if you already own one, runs in a single transaction so a failed debit can't half-credit the slot. `services/crafting.py:add_specialty` now reads the per-user extra_slots column when checking the cap, and the error message points at `,shop buy specialty_slot` when capped.

### NFT layer Phase 2 PR7: ore stays fungible + multi-qty AH escrow + `,admin nft reconcile`
- **Design call: ore stays fungible**. `COPPER` / `SILVER` / `GOLD` keep living in `wallet_holdings` with oracle prices, stake yields, and AMM trades. Per-unit NFT semantics break the fractional-amount + economic-currency model. The `ore.*` contracts are removed from the `nft_bootstrap` deploy plan and the (already no-op) ore backfill is dropped from the `run_backfill` plan. Existing ore listings in the AH (legacy `_lock_ore` path) still target wallet_holdings; that's a separate AH-side bug if any guilds were trying to list ore.
- **Multi-qty AH escrow now uses N tokens**: migration `0178` adds `auction_listing_tokens (listing_id, token_id)` join table. `services/auction.py:create_listing` now escrows `qty` oldest-first per-unit tokens (one per listed unit) and writes one join row per token. `cancel_listing` and `buy_listing` sweep ownership across every joined token. `auction_listings.token_id` stays as the "primary" token (always the first of the N) for backward compat with the existing FK; the bundle metadata lives on the listing row as before. Backfill: every existing listing gets one join row pointing at its primary token.
- **`,admin nft reconcile`**: new admin command in `cogs/admin.py` backed by `services/nft_reconcile.py`. Diffs JSONB / scalar inventory counts vs unburned token counts per `(user_id, kind, catalog_key)`. Empty drift report = NFT shadow is in sync; safe to flip reads. Drift rows show jsonb_count vs nft_count and which side is ahead. Optional `@user` arg scopes to a single player. This is the gate to clear before swapping cog reads from JSONB to `count_owned()`.

### NFT layer Phase 2 PR6: player-facing `,nft` commands
- **`,nft`**: overview embed -- count of every unburned NFT you own grouped by kind.
- **`,nft list [kind]`**: list owned tokens grouped by contract (so 50 worm bait collapses to one line). Optional kind filter for buddy / egg / fish / crop / bait / junk / weapon / armor / consumable / crafted / stone / shop / ore.
- **`,nft inspect <token_id>`**: full details for a single token -- contract address, network, owner / escrow / burn status, mint source + time, and any non-default metadata captured at mint (lbs for fish, gender for buddies, level + staked for stones, etc.).
- **`,nft contracts [kind]`**: catalog of every deployed contract (one per item type the bot knows how to mint). Adding an item to a config dict deploys its contract on the next boot via `services/nft_bootstrap.py`.
- **`,nft contract <address>`**: detail view for one contract -- supply stats (alive / burned / total minted) plus how many you personally own.
- **`,nft transfer <token_id> @user`**: gift a token to another player. Pure NFT transfer -- the underlying inventory row (cc_buddies record, JSONB count) is NOT moved, so this is intended for the collectible flow alongside the cog-specific gift commands (`,fish egg gift`, etc.) and the auction house. Refuses self-gifts, bots, escrowed tokens, burned tokens, and cross-server attempts.

### NFT layer Phase 2 PR5: consume + transfer for guards, stones, buddies
- **`use_validator_guard` / `use_yield_guard`** in `database/users.py` now call `items.consume_one('shop.<id>')` after the JSONB / inventory decrement, so activating a guard burns the corresponding NFT.
- **Stone level-up** in `cogs/shop.py:_buy_stone` (level-up branch) now refreshes the existing `stone.<key>` token's metadata (`level`, `staked`) instead of minting a new one. Stone tokens stay 1:1 with the underlying stone row across every level.
- **Buddy surrender** in `services/buddy_lifecycle.py:to_shelter` clears `owner_user_id` on the buddy token so shelter buddies have no NFT owner until adoption.
- **Buddy adopt** in `try_adopt` and **buddy reclaim** in `try_reclaim` call `items.transfer(token_id, new_owner)` to move the buddy NFT to its new home.
- **Ore parked**: the `ore.*` contracts are still deployed but no per-unit mint runs at credit time. Ore amounts are fractional (`qty_human=float` in `_credit_ore`) so unit semantics don't fit. Decision pending: treat ore as fungible (current path -- lives in `wallet_holdings`) or floor() the qty and lose the fractional remainder. Leaving the existing wallet path untouched until you call the design.

### NFT layer Phase 2 PR4: AH listing reuses existing per-unit token (no duplicate mint)
- **`services/auction.py:create_listing` no longer lazy-mints a duplicate token** when the seller already has a per-unit token for the listed item. New `_resolve_token_for_listing` helper looks up the seller's oldest owned token under `(<kind>.<catalog_key>)` via `items.list_owned`, escrows it (`owner_user_id = NULL`), and uses its `token_id` on the listing. Falls back to the legacy `mint_token` path when no contract exists yet (pre-Phase-1 items, items the bootstrap missed). For multi-qty listings the primary listing token stays a single row -- the qty + metadata still represent the bundle -- so cancel/buy keep working unchanged. The remaining qty-1 NFT tokens stay with the seller this phase; routing them through the AH ships in a later PR alongside the JSONB-counter retirement.

### NFT layer Phase 2 PR3: crafting + shop wired through `services/items`
- **Crafting**: `services/crafting.py:craft_item` mints one `crafted.<key>` token per produced unit; `_decrement_crafted` (the consumption helper for `,craft apply`) burns one token per consumed unit. `_apply_to_fishing_bait` mints `bait.<key>` tokens when a craft converts to bait so the same kind never has two source-of-truth paths.
- **Shop stones + consumables**: `cogs/shop.py:_buy_stone` mints a `stone.<key>` token per purchased stone (one stone per player, so always unit_index=1 unless backfill ran first). `_buy_consumable` mints a `shop.<item_id>` token per purchased validator_guard / yield_guard. Stone level-up + consumable use paths still need consume sites (PR4 follow-up).
- **Phase 2 remaining**: stone level-up burn, charm / save consume, AH listing flow looking up existing tokens (today the AH still lazy-mints a duplicate via `mint_token` for items that were created post-Phase-1).

### NFT layer Phase 2 PR2: farming + dungeon wired through `services/items`
- **Farming**: `services/farming.py:harvest_plot` mints one `crop.<key>` token per harvested unit; `sell_crop` burns one token per unit sold; `process_recipe` burns one token per consumed raw crop. Best-effort sync alongside the existing JSONB writes (JSONB stays source of truth).
- **Dungeon**: `services/dungeon.py:buy_item` mints one `weapon.<key>` / `armor.<key>` / `consumable.<key>` token per purchase. `mine_action` burns one `consumable.pickaxe_oil` token when the buff is consumed. Wild-mob capture mints a `buddy.<species>` token for the captured opponent.
- **Ore backfill is a no-op for now**: ore (COPPER / SILVER / GOLD) lives in `wallet_holdings` as fungible token symbols, not as scalar columns on `user_dungeon`, so the per-unit NFT semantics need a design call (treat as currency vs. mint per unit). The `ore.*` contracts are still deployed by the bootstrap so a future runtime mint can attach to them. The backfill helper now returns 0 cleanly instead of querying phantom `*_qty` columns.

### NFT layer Phase 2 PR1: fishing cog wired through `services/items`
- **Bait consumption on cast burns one bait token**: `services/fishing.py:begin_cast` decrements the JSONB counter as before AND calls `items.consume_one(contract='bait.<key>')` so the on-chain count tracks the JSONB. JSONB is still the source of truth for read paths this PR; the NFT side runs in shadow + best-effort so a registry hiccup never costs a player their cast.
- **Fish + junk catches mint a per-unit token**: `services/fishing.py:cast_resolve` now calls `items.mint_unit(contract='fish.<key>', metadata={lbs, ts, rarity, zone})` for every caught fish entry and `items.mint_unit(contract='junk.<key>')` for every junk pull, right after the JSONB UPDATE + `record_catch`. Each fish entry is its own token (matches the per-entry shape of `fish_inventory[fish_key]`).
- **Bait shop buy mints N tokens**: `services/fishing.py:buy_bait` mints one `bait.<key>` token per actual unit purchased after the JSONB UPDATE.
- **Fish + junk sell burns tokens**: `services/fishing.py:sell_inventory` calls `items.consume_one` for every fish/junk unit sold so the burned-at column tracks consumption history.
- **Egg create / hatch / sell / gift / wild-loot all wire through the NFT layer**:
  - Held-egg create (shelter-full path in `hatch_fishing_buddy`, `give_held_egg`, wild-battle loot drop) mints `egg.<species>` tokens.
  - Direct hatch and held-egg hatch mint `buddy.<species>` tokens for the new buddy and burn the corresponding `egg.<species>` token.
  - `sell_held_eggs` burns one `egg.<species>` per consumed egg.
  - `gift_held_eggs` transfers one egg token per gifted egg from sender to recipient through `items.transfer`.
  - Wild-battle capture mints a `buddy.<species>` token for the captured wild buddy.
- **Phase 2 PR2+ remaining**: farming/dungeon/crafting/shop/buddy create+consume paths, plus a follow-up to make the auction-house listing flow look up the existing per-unit token instead of lazy-minting a new one (which currently produces a duplicate token row when a player lists an item created post-Phase-1).

### NFT layer Phase 1: per-unit tokens + contract registry + backfill
- **Real contract registry (`item_contracts`) + per-unit `item_instances`**: Migration 0176 promotes the lazy auction-only `item_instances` table into a full per-unit NFT layer. Every item type the bot can mint (every buddy species, every fish, every bait, every weapon / armor / consumable / crafted item, every stone, every shop item) becomes a row in `item_contracts` with a stable address shaped `<kind>.<catalog_key>` (e.g. `bait.worm`, `weapon.bronze_sword`, `egg.zenny`, `buddy.zenny`). `item_instances` gains `contract_id` (FK), `unit_index` (per-contract serial), `minted_at` / `burned_at` / `mint_source` so each unit is individually addressable and the ledger stays append-only on consume.
- **Catalog-walking deploy at startup**: `services/nft_bootstrap.py:deploy_all_contracts(db)` runs once per boot, walks every catalog dict (`buddies_config.SPECIES`, `fishing_config.BAIT/FISH/JUNK`, `farming_config.CROPS`, `dungeon_config.WEAPONS/ARMOR/CONSUMABLES`, `crafting_config.CRAFT_ITEMS`, `items_config.SHOP_ITEMS`), and idempotently upserts a contract row per entry. Adding a new item to a config file is enough to "deploy" its contract on the next boot.
- **One-shot backfill**: `services/nft_backfill.py:run_backfill(db)` mints a per-unit token for every existing unit in every inventory table -- buddies (1:1), held eggs (1 per JSONB entry), fish inventory (1 per catch entry), ore (N tokens for N qty in `copper_qty`/`silver_qty`/`gold_qty`), and every count-map JSONB inventory (`bait_inventory`, `junk_inventory`, `crop_inventory`, `weapons_owned`, `armor_owned`, `consumables`, `crafted_inventory`). Checkpointed via `nft_backfill_state` so reruns only retry kinds that failed; per-row idempotency check (`source_table` + `source_id` already minted?) guards partial-failure reruns from double-minting. A `_link_existing` pass also retro-fits `contract_id` + `unit_index` onto any pre-Phase-1 `item_instances` rows that the auction house had lazy-minted before the registry existed.
- **New `services/items.py` API**: `contract_address(kind, key)`, `get_contract()`, `upsert_contract()`, `list_contracts()`, `mint_unit()` (allocates a fresh per-contract unit_index, deterministic token_id from `(network, contract_address, unit_index)`), `burn_unit(token_id, reason=)` (append-only burn), `consume_one()` (FIFO burn the oldest owned unit of a contract -- the building block for "use 1 worm bait" flows in Phase 2), `count_owned()`, `list_owned()`. The legacy `mint_token()` still works for in-flight auction code paths; Phase 2 will replace its callers with `mint_unit`.
- **Phase 2 (next PRs) is the cog wiring**: every place an item is currently created (catch, mine, harvest, craft, shop buy, drop) needs to mint via `mint_unit` instead of incrementing a JSONB counter; every consume path needs to call `consume_one`. Auction flows will switch to looking up an existing token (no new mint) and transferring ownership. This will land cog-by-cog so any one shape change can be reverted independently.

## [main] -- 2026-04-29

### Buddy gender + breeding pair requirement
- **Every buddy now has a gender (♂ / ♀)**: Migration `0174` adds a NOT NULL `cc_buddies.gender TEXT CHECK (gender IN ('M', 'F'))` column with a per-row 50/50 random backfill so existing buddies don't end up ungendered after the upgrade. New buddies roll a fresh 50/50 gender at every creation point: fishing direct-hatch, fishing held-egg drop, fishing immediate-hatch, dungeon mob capture, farming wild capture, daycare collect, `,buddy hatch`, and `,buddy reroll`. There's a `cc_buddies (guild_id, owner_user_id, gender)` index ready for any future "find a breeding partner" leaderboard / picker.
- **Held eggs carry a pre-rolled gender too**: `held_eggs[].gender` is set at the moment the egg lands so the player sees what they'd hatch BEFORE they hatch it (`,fish egg` now prints the ♂ / ♀ glyph next to each per-egg index). Migration `0174` also adds a NOT NULL `cc_buddy_daycare.egg_gender` column with the same backfill so any in-progress daycare slots survive cleanly. Legacy held-egg rows that pre-date the migration roll a fresh gender at hatch time so no buddy ever inherits a NULL.
- **Daycare requires one ♂ + one ♀**: `,buddy daycare deposit` now refuses two of the same gender with a clear error showing which glyph each picked parent has, so the player can swap. Egg roll at deposit time picks species (50/50 from the parents), rarity (existing inherit weights), AND a fresh 50/50 gender; the collect path threads that through `give_held_egg(gender=...)` so the held-egg row matches what the daycare advertised.
- **Gender visible everywhere a buddy or egg shows up**: ♂ / ♀ glyph now renders on `,buddy stats` / `,buddy info` / `,buddy me` (right after the name in the title), `,buddy storage` rows, the `,me` shelter card, the `,fish egg` per-egg index list, every `,ah browse` row for buddy and egg listings, and `,ah inspect` / `,ah token` detail panels. Glyph maps to canonical 'M' / 'F' codes via `buddies_config.gender_glyph()`; the Unicode never touches the data layer.
- **`,ah list egg <species>:<gender>` and `<species>:<tier>:<gender>`**: Egg ref parser now accepts a gender filter alongside the existing tier filter. Examples: `,ah list egg wecco:F 5000` (your female wecco), `,ah list egg wecco:legendary:M 5000` (your male legendary wecco), `,ah list egg wecco:M:T5 5000` (order doesn't matter). Gender accepts `M` / `F` / `male` / `female` / `boy` / `girl` / ♂ / ♀. The error path now prints a tier+gender breakdown of what you actually hold so you can copy a valid token straight out of the message.

### Auction-house bug fixes + UX
- **`,ah list <kind> ...` no longer dies with "could not list that item"**: The auction service was wrapping its writes in ``db.transaction() as conn`` and then calling ``conn.fetch_one(...)`` / ``db.fetch_one(...)`` (where ``db`` was the raw asyncpg connection). Asyncpg's Connection object exposes ``fetchrow`` / ``fetch``, NOT the repo wrapper's ``fetch_one`` / ``fetch_all`` -- so every list/cancel/buy/expire call was raising ``AttributeError`` and getting eaten by the cog's catch-all ``except Exception`` handler that prints the generic "could not list that item -- try again." Switched all four sites (``create_listing`` / ``cancel_listing`` / ``buy_listing`` / ``expire_old``) to ``async with db.atomic():`` -- the codebase's contextvar pattern that pins every ``db.*`` call inside the block to the same pooled connection so the helpers' API surface (``fetch_one`` / ``fetch_all`` / ``fetch_val`` / ``execute``) keeps working. The handler signatures already took ``db: Any`` so the lock/return/deliver triples didn't need touching.
- **List eggs by `<species>:<tier>` -- target a specific rarity**: `,ah list egg wecco:legendary 5000` lists your Legendary wecco specifically, leaving any Common / Rare wecco eggs untouched. `,ah list egg crab:T3 1500` works too (tier accepts ``T1``..``T5`` / ``1``..``5`` / ``leg`` / ``epi`` / ``rar`` / ``unc`` / ``com`` / full names like ``legendary``). With no tier, ``,ah list egg wecco 5000`` still picks the highest-rarity match. Bare numeric `,ah list egg 0 5000` still works for the explicit per-egg index.
- **List buddies by NAME, not just id**: `,ah list buddy Sparky 50000` now works alongside `,ah list buddy 1234 50000`. Name lookup is case-insensitive exact-match; if multiple buddies share the same name the highest-level one wins (usually the player's main).
- **`,fish egg` shows per-egg indices**: New "Each egg (use idx with `,ah list egg`)" field lists every held egg with its ``#N`` index, species, and rarity tier, sorted by rarity desc / species asc so the legendary you want isn't buried under common dupes. The summary "By species + rarity" field is preserved for at-a-glance counts. Field auto-chunks past ~20 eggs to stay under Discord's 1024-char-per-field cap.
- **Buddy panel surfaces the buddy id in the title**: `,buddy stats` / `,buddy info` / `,buddy me` titles now read `🐟  Sparky  ·  #1234` so a player can copy the id straight into `,ah list buddy 1234 <price>` / `,buddy store 1234` / `,buddy reroll 1234` without bouncing into a separate command.
- **`,ah list` help text rewritten with the new ref formats**: Added concrete examples for buddy-id, buddy-name, egg-index, egg-species, and egg-species:tier paths plus a "Ref formats" section in `,ah help`. Egg lock errors now print a tier-aware breakdown of what you actually hold (`2x wecco:legendary, 1x crab:rare, ...`) instead of just species counts.

### Auction-house consolidation
- **`,ah` is now the categorised browser**: Bare `,ah` opens an interactive panel showing every active listing in the guild, bucketed by kind (Buddies / Eggs / Fish / Crops / Ore / Weapons / Armor / Consumables / Crafted). Embed colour tints to the active filter so a fish-only browse reads teal, a buddy-only browse reads purple, etc. -- the player asked for colours, the player gets colours.
- **Dropdown filter + sort cycle + Prev/Next buttons**: The browser is owner-locked with a 5-min timeout. The dropdown swaps kinds in place; the Sort button cycles `newest` -> `cheapest` -> `expensive` -> `expiring` -> `newest`; Prev / Next page through up to 200 listings (8 per page); Refresh re-fetches so newly-listed items appear immediately.
- **`,ah search <text>`**: New free-text search across the user-facing `ref`, the buddy `name`, the egg `species`, and the NFT-style `token_id` (full or 8-char short form). Case-insensitive substring match. `,ah search wecco` finds every wecco egg / buddy; `,ah search bud:k889ka2c` jumps straight to a token. Aliases: `,ah find` / `,ah lookup`.
- **`,ah browse [kind]` shares the same view**: The keyword-only `--max=` flag is gone (use Sort -> cheapest instead), but `--sort=cheapest|expensive|expiring|newest` still works as a quick-pre-filter. Aliases: `view` / `all` / `catalog`.
- **`,ah list egg` accepts species name OR numeric index**: `,ah list egg wecco 5000` now picks your highest-rarity wecco automatically (tiebreak by rarity desc); `,ah list egg 0 5000` still works for the explicit index. The error path lists every species you hold + counts so you can see what's listable without leaving chat.
- **Legacy `,buddy market` / `,buddy mylistings` / `,buddy list` / `,buddy egg list` / `,buddy egg market` are now redirect stubs**: Each prints a one-card "moved to the auction house" panel with the exact `,ah ...` command for the same operation. The old `cc_buddy_listings` table is left intact; `,buddy buy` and `,buddy delist` remain functional so any in-flight legacy listings can still settle, but their error paths now point at `,ah buy` / `,ah cancel` for the corresponding listing id.
- **Embed copy + help cleanup**: `,fish egg` empty-state, `,fish egg` footer, `,fish egg` help-field, `,start` shop hub, the buddy shelter card on `,me`, and the `,help auction` page all now reference `,ah` (no more dangling pointers to the deprecated buddy market).

### Gap-fill pass
- **Buyer DM on `,ah buy`**: Sellers were already getting a DM on settle; now buyers get a symmetric purchase receipt (token id + listed-vs-paid + slippage note when cross-currency). Best-effort -- closed DMs log and move on.
- **`,ah history`**: Settled-trade log -- one embed showing every listing where you were the seller (sold / cancelled / expired) AND every listing where you were the buyer (sold), newest first up to 50. Per-row glyph differentiates `\U0001F4B0 sold` / `\U0001F6CD bought` / `\U000026D4 cancelled` / `\U000023F0 expired`. Header surfaces totals.
- **`,ah inspect` accepts token id OR listing id**: `,ah inspect 17` works, `,ah inspect bud:k889ka2c` works. Token-id route falls through to `,ah token` when the item isn't actively listed so the inspect command always lands somewhere useful.
- **`,ah browse` filter + sort flags**: `--max=NNN` caps the listed price (in the listed currency); `--sort=` accepts `newest` / `cheapest` / `expensive` / `expiring`. Combinable: `,ah browse buddy --max=10000 --sort=cheapest`.
- **5 auction-house achievements**: New `auction` category with **Open for Business** (first listing), **First Buck** (first sale), **Window Shopper** (first purchase), **Currency Arbitrageur** (first cross-currency buy), **Seasoned Seller** (100 settled sales). Bus events `ah_listing_created` / `ah_sale_settled` / `ah_purchase_settled` / `ah_cross_currency_buy` are published from the cog and subscribed by `services/achievements.py` + `services/quests.py` (so a future quest pool can ask "list 3 items today" without re-plumbing).
- **Auction House section in the `,start` Guide tab**: New player opening the Guide tab now sees the marketplace alongside Fishing / Farming / Dungeon / Crafting / Buddies / Arena. Quick-action buttons gain an Auction shortcut to `,help auction`.
- **`,buddy market` points at the auction house**: Header on the legacy buddy/egg market embed now mentions `,ah` as the cross-game equivalent so players discover the new system without losing the old flow. The buddy market still works -- it's a soft pointer, not a removal.



### New Features
- **Auction House: list and buy any item kind**: New `,ah` command group (aliases `,auction` / `,market` / `,ahouse`) replaces the buddy-only market with a generic listings table that takes any item kind: buddies, eggs, fish, crops, ore, weapons, armors, consumables, crafted items. List one item or a stack with `,ah list <kind> <ref> [qty] <price> [currency] [--ttl=days]`; browse the catalog with `,ah browse [kind]`; purchase with `,ah buy <id> [pay_currency]`; cancel your own with `,ah cancel <id>`. Each listing defaults its currency to the kind's home network coin (buddy/egg -> BUD, fish -> LURE, crop -> HRV, ore/weapon/armor/consumable -> RUNE, crafted -> INGOT) but sellers can override. Direct purchases in the listed currency settle peer-to-peer; cross-currency purchases auto-route through the AMM with **real impact** (the same `_price_impact` formula every other swap surface uses, scaling with USD value vs market cap). House fee is **5%** of sale price, burned as a sink. Listings expire after **7 days** by default (overridable with `--ttl=N`); a 5-minute background sweep auto-returns expired-listing items to the seller and DMs them. Sellers also get a DM the moment a listing settles. Per-user cap of **25 active listings**.
- **NFT-style token IDs for every listed item**: New `item_instances` table assigns each ownable item a stable identifier formatted `<network>:<hex>` -- e.g. **bud:k889ka2c** (a buddy), **reel:81819ab9** (a fish), **hrv:af09c12e** (a crop), **rune:b3d201c5** (an ore stack), **fge:9931ee2a** (a crafted item). The hex is content-derived (BLAKE2b over salt + network + source_table + source_id) so the same source row always resolves to the same token id across restarts. Items "bought with USD" (buddies) inherit their closest related crypto network (BUD). New `,ah token <id>` looks up any minted token even when it isn't currently listed (e.g. a buddy that's been sitting in your shelter for weeks), surfaces kind / network / current owner / kind-specific extras, and points to the active listing if there is one. The token layer is generic: any future cross-game ownership / NFT export / off-chain bridge plugs in without schema churn.
- **Migration `0173`**: Adds `item_instances` (token_id PK + network + kind + source ref + owner + listing fk + metadata JSONB) and `auction_listings` (id PK + token_id FK + seller + qty + currency + price_raw + status + auction_fee_bps + listed/expires/settled/cancelled timestamps). Both tables come with hot-path indexes on the active-browse / by-seller / expiring-soon paths.
- **`cogs/auction.py`** (~600 lines) wires the command surface: `list / browse / buy / cancel / mine / sold / inspect / token / help`, plus an in-cog `_expire_loop` background task that sweeps expired listings every 5 min and DMs sellers. **`services/auction.py`** (~750 lines) owns the per-kind escrow handlers, settlement transactions, real-impact cross-currency conversion, and the `expire_old` sweep entrypoint. **`services/items.py`** (~180 lines) exposes the token-id layer.
- **Capture button on delve wild buddy battles**: A `Capture (NN%)` button now appears alongside Strike / Special / Brace / Risky in the wild-buddy battle view. Disabled while enemy HP > the standard `CAPTURE_HP_THRESHOLD` (30%); enables below it with a live percentage on the label. Capture chance scales with how low HP is plus the rarity-tier penalty. Successful captures insert the buddy into `cc_buddies`, finalise the battle as a captured win, AND publish the `delve_wild_buddy_captured` bus event so achievements / quests / challenges credit it. The post-finalize auto-capture roll is skipped via a new `skip_capture_roll` kwarg on `services.dungeon.resolve_wild_battle` so the manual + auto paths can never double-insert.
- **Five cheese recipes added to the cooking track**: A fresh wedge of buddy treats so a Cook actually has a flavour identity. Two general-tier (anyone can craft, off-spec gets the 10% XP rate): **🧀 Curd Wheel** (L1 common, `buddy/feed`, 2 FGD) and **🧀 Sharp Cheddar** (L5 uncommon, `buddy/feed`, 14 FGD). Three specialty-locked for dedicated cooks: **🧀 Smoked Gouda** (L13 rare, `buddy/feast` so the whole shelter eats, 70 FGD), **🧀 Bleu Cheese** (L23 epic, `buddy/restore` for full mood reset, 380 FGD), and **🧀 Truffle Brie** (L40 legendary, `buddy/feast`, 4,500 FGD). Inputs are crop+ore-heavy for the cheap end and grow into kraken-tier fish + GOLD + FREN for the legendary, mirroring the existing rarity ramp; outputs reuse already-implemented buddy effects so no integration-side changes are needed.

### Changes
- **Off-specialty crafts now grant 10% XP (10x slower) instead of 50%**: Going wide is still possible -- the aggregate crafting level AND the recipe's specialty XP both still tick when a generalist crafts an off-spec recipe -- but the climb is dramatically slower so picking a specialty is the obvious play. Specialist-locked recipes (`requires_specialty: True`) remain uncraftable until the matching branch is in your active set; this multiplier only governs the general-tier recipes. `,craft specialties` text updated to spell out the new rate and the "still levels you up, just slowly" guarantee.
- **`,craft list` / `,craft info` / `,craft book` redesigned with code-block tables, rarity dots, and clean general/specialist delineation**: Each surface now opens with a wallet + active-specialties + rarity-legend header, then renders recipes in two clearly-labeled top-level sections -- 🔓 GENERAL RECIPES (anyone can craft) and 🔒 SPECIALIST RECIPES (need the matching branch). General recipes group by downstream game (Fishing bait / Farming fertilizer / Dungeon consumables / Buddy treats); specialist recipes group by branch (Smithing / Alchemy / etc.) with an "active" / "locked" tag per branch. Every recipe row lives in a column-aligned code-block table (Lvl / Rarity abbrev / FGD / key / name) so two recipes are head-to-head comparable at a glance. Rarity tier shows as a coloured dot (🟤 com / 🟢 unc / 🔵 rar / 🟣 epi / 🟡 leg) plus the three-letter abbrev in the table. `,craft info` switches its inputs to a `Qty / Ingredient / Source` table so the player sees exactly where to grind each ingredient without leaving the embed; the costs/yields field becomes its own aligned mini-table. `,craft book` no longer paginates -- per-category truncation ("...and N more in this category.") keeps the entire catalog on one embed; players hop into specifics with `,craft info <key>` or filter the book with `,craft book <specialty>`. Locked recipes get an `L` (level-gated) / `S` (specialty-locked) marker in the leading column so you can see what's craftable right now without parsing prose.

### Bug Fixes
- **`,help <token symbol>` now works for every coin in the game**: Typing `,help ingot`, `,help forge`, `,help fgd`, `,help reel`, `,help rune`, `,help bud`, `,help hrv`, etc. used to return "Unknown category" because none of those symbols were aliased to a topic. New `_TOKEN_TOPIC` map routes every known token (earn-only + network coin + stablecoin) to its relevant help page -- INGOT/FORGE/FGD now land on the Crafting page, REEL/LURE on Fishing, RUNE/ore on Dungeon, etc. Tokens without a dedicated game page (BUD/FREN/BBT/USDC/DSD/etc.) route to the currencies cheatsheet which already has a per-network section. Map covers all 23 tokens currently defined in `Config.TOKENS`.
- **Crafting help expanded with proper INGOT / FORGE / FGD explainers**: The `,help crafting` page (also reachable via `,help forge` / `,help ingot` / `,help fgd` / each specialty name) had a single tight 8-line "Token economy" field that listed the commands but never explained what each token actually was. Replaced with three dedicated fields -- 🧱 INGOT (the crafting reward token: how it's earned, mint range, what to stake/swap/cashout), 🔨 FORGE (the network coin: only inflows are stake yield + burn-swap, only off-ramp is cashout), 💵 FGD (the $1-pegged fee currency: how to buy with USD, where it's used). Aliases added: `craft / forge / smith / smithing / ingot / fgd / alchemy / cooking / fletching / tinkering / enchanting` all route to the same expanded page so a player can land on it from whatever name comes to mind.
- **`,fish inv` no longer crashes for big haulers**: The fish field crammed up to 25 entries into a single field, each ~120 chars; anyone with a deep tackle box hit `400 Bad Request: Must be 1024 or fewer in length`. Inventory rendering now chunks each section (Fish / Junk / Bait / Crab Traps) into 1000-char field shards labeled "(cont.)" on overflow, and packs those shards across multiple embeds (5000-char body budget, 24 fields each) when the whole haul exceeds Discord's 6000-char-per-embed ceiling. Single embed -> `,send_embed`; multi-page -> `ctx.paginate`. New `_chunk_lines_to_fields` helper is reusable for any other sectioned inventory that grows.
- **`,start` Stones tab is now wired up**: Tab was declared in `_TAB_KEYS` but never had a fetch / render / actions implementation, so `,start` -> Stones rendered the placeholder "This tab is not wired up yet". New tab pulls every owned stone from the nine `get_<stone>` DB getters (Hashstone / Lockstone / Vaultstone / Liqstone / Tidestone / Heartstone / Cryptstone / Bloodstone / Bloomstone), shows level + staked amount + currency for owned ones and "not yet  ·  buy with X" for the rest. Auto-levelup status is in the summary line and toggleable from a context-sensitive button (Auto-up ON / OFF). Quick actions: Inventory / Shop / Auto-up / Stones help.
- **`,me` and `,start` fishing tabs no longer say "no activity yet"**: Both surfaces queried `user_fishing` for column names that hadn't existed since the early migrations -- `level` / `xp` / `biggest_catch_lbs` / `biggest_catch_value`. The actual columns are `fish_level` / `fish_xp` / `biggest_lbs` (per migration `0132_fishing.sql`). The query threw `UndefinedColumnError`, the except-handler swallowed it, and the section/tab fell back to the empty placeholder. Fixed both call sites to use the canonical names; the showcase's farming tab had the same bug (`crafting_level` instead of `farm_level` / `farm_xp`) and is fixed in the same pass.
- **`,mylp` no longer crashes for users with many LP positions**: Single-embed render packed every position into one card; players with enough liquidity to push the total past Discord's 6000-char-per-embed ceiling got `400 Bad Request: Embed size exceeds maximum size of 6000` instead of their portfolio. Per-position fields are now greedy-packed across multiple embeds (5000-char body budget per page, max 20 positions per page) and `,paginate` carousels them. Yield Summary lands on the last page; the Total LP value footer renders on every page so the headline number is always visible. Per-field values are also defensively truncated to 1020 chars so a single verbose row can never trip the 1024-char field cap either.
- **`,start` tab wallet balances no longer read zero on Fishing / Farming / Delve**: The tab fetchers passed the wrong network-short codes to `db.get_wallet_holding` -- `"lure"` / `"harvest"` / `"crypt"` instead of the canonical `"lur"` / `"har"` / `"cry"` (see `fishing_config.LURE_NETWORK_SHORT`, `farming_config.HARVEST_NETWORK_SHORT`, `dungeon_config.CRYPT_NETWORK_SHORT`). The query filters on the `network` column, so passing the longer string returned `None` for every player and the tab rendered LURE / REEL / HRV / RUNE balances as $0. Fixed all three lookups; Buddy and Crafting tabs were already correct (`"bud"` / `"fge"`).
- **`,changelog` now shows entries from `--`-separated date headers**: The parser regex only matched a single dash character (em / en / one ASCII hyphen) between the `[main]` tag and the date, so newer entries that used `--` (the project's current style per the project guidelines "no fancy dashes" rule) were silently skipped. The bot would render the latest available em-dash entry (04-25 / 04-23 / etc.) and pretend nothing had shipped on 04-26 or 04-29. Regex now accepts either `--` or any of the single-dash forms; both old (em dash) and new (`--`) entries render. 04-29 alone surfaces ~30 previously-invisible entries.

### New Features
- **Cheese branch added to Cooking**: Four new cooking recipes (Fresh Cheese / Aged Cheddar / Blue Round / Moonmilk Brie) spanning common -> epic. Fresh Cheese is general (anyone), the rest are Cooking-specialty-locked. Effects mirror the existing buddy treats (feed / restore / xp_big) so the food category is wired into the same apply paths.
- **Best-in-game weapon + armor as legendary Smithing recipes**: `soul_reaver_forge` and `first_skin_forge` -- both Lv 50, Smithing-locked, requiring ~1.4k ore + Leviathan/Kraken catches + 1k FREN + ~25k FGD per craft. Output mints the actual T11 Soul Reaver (+500 ATK) and First Skin (+360 DEF) directly into `user_dungeon.weapons_owned` / `armor_owned` so the player can equip them with `,delve equip`. New `weapon/<key>` and `armor/<key>` apply kinds added to `services.crafting._apply_to_dungeon_*`. Stack cap is 1 -- strictly endgame, no farming for spares.
- **Capture button on delve wild-buddy battles**: Wild fights in `,delve` now show a **Capture (NN%)** button on row 1 alongside Strike / Special / Brace / Risky. Disabled while enemy HP > `CAPTURE_HP_THRESHOLD` (30%); enables below it with a live percentage on the label so the player can read the chance and decide whether to throw or wear them down further. Capture chance scales with how low HP is plus the standard rarity-tier penalty (`CAPTURE_BASE_CHANCE - tier_penalty + (1 - hp_frac/threshold) * 0.5`). On success the wild buddy is inserted into `cc_buddies` immediately and the battle finalises as a captured win (mirrors the regular mob `btn_capture` shape); on failure the wild buddy gets a free turn and the fight continues.

### Bug Fixes
- **AI no longer says "[redacted]" when referencing channels**: `core.framework.ai.safety._MENTION_RE` blanket-redacted `<#channel_id>` mentions, so when Disco said "head over to <#1234>" the sanitizer scrubbed it to "[redacted]". Channel mentions don't ping anyone -- they just render as a clickable link -- so the redaction was wrong. Split into a separate `_OUTPUT_MENTION_RE` that drops only the things that actually ping (`@everyone` / `@here` / user / role); channel mentions pass through cleanly. Input + context-snippet sanitisation still scrubs channel ids since the model doesn't need to see them upstream.
- **`,admin botchannel clear` and `,admin aichannel clear`**: Admins now have a one-shot wipe path for the bot-channel allowlist and the AI ambient-chat allowlist. Accepts `clear` / `reset` / `wipe` / `none` / `all`. New `clear_bot_channels()` / `clear_ai_chat_channels()` helpers on `database/guilds.py` return the count of entries removed so the reply confirms what was nuked. List-view footer now mentions the clear path.

### New Features (cont.)
- **Crafting specialties: pick-2 with locked recipes + bonuses**: The five-track specialty system gains a sixth branch (**Enchanting** -- runes, fortune, oracle effects) and a real selection mechanic. Players hold up to **2 active specialties** at a time via `,craft specialize <key>` / `,craft despecialize <key>`. New `requires_specialty: True` recipes only craft while that specialty is in your active set; in-specialty crafts get **+1% INGOT mint per specialty level** (so a Lv 50 Alchemist nets +50% INGOT on every alchemy craft they own); off-specialty crafts pay **50% XP** so going wide is possible but slow. **21 new recipes** ship: 3 specialty-locked recipes per branch (one common-tier accessible / one rare / one legendary, 18 total) plus 5 new general-tier recipes that anyone can craft. Migration `0172` adds `active_specialties TEXT[]` (with a CHECK enforcing the 2-pick cap) and the `enchanting_xp / enchanting_level` columns. New `,craft book [specialty]` recipe browser shows every recipe in the catalog with **material sources per ingredient** (fishing / farming / dungeon / wallet), full input lists, FGD fee, INGOT mint range, XP, and a 🔒 lock marker against any recipe gated by level or specialty pick. `,craft list` and `,craft info` also surface the lock state.
- **New `Guide` tab on `,start`**: Centralised cheatsheet for every minigame (Fishing / Farming / Dungeon / Crafting / Buddies / Arena) packed into one tab, sequenced in rough onboarding order. Each section is a 30-second playbook -- "what to do, what you earn, how to cash out" -- so a new player sees the whole game economy on one screen instead of having to discover six separate `,help` pages. Slot `,fish stake` / `,farm stake` / `,delve stake` / etc. into context with the right token names. Quick-action buttons jump straight to `,help fishing` / `,help farming` / `,help dungeon` / `,help crafting` / `,help bud` for the deeper reference. Tab sits right after Home in the dropdown so it's the first thing a new player can click after the dashboard.
- **`,farm inv` / `,farm inventory` aliases**: `,farm bag` already showed crops + seeds + fertilizer + processed goods; the same data is now reachable via `,farm inv` / `,farm inventory` / `,farm tacklebox` for parity with `,fish inv`. Same renderer, no new code path.
- **`,start` dashboard surfaces every new feature**: The tabbed `,start` interface now exposes the buddy storage / daycare and crafting work shipped on this branch. New **Crafting** tab (alongside Buddy / Fishing / Farming / Delve / etc.) shows aggregate crafting level + per-specialty levels (Smithing / Alchemy / Cooking / Fletching / Tinkering), INGOT stake state, FORGE / FGD wallet, and a Claim button that only appears when there's pending FORGE yield. Buddy tab gains a Storage + Daycare summary line (stored count, daycare timer / "egg ready") and adds **Storage** + **Daycare** quick-action buttons. Game-hub buddy submenu gains the same two buttons; new **Crafting** game in the hub root with Forge / Recipes / Specialties / Stake / Leaderboard quick actions. Home tab "Next Steps" now suggests "Forge your first craft" once the player has 5+ fish / 5+ crops / 1+ delve run, "Stash a spare buddy" once they own 2+ buddies, and "Breed a new buddy in the daycare" once 2+ buddies are owned. Progress checklist gains a Crafting line. State gather adds `total_crafts`, `n_owned_buddies`, `n_stored_buddies`, `daycare_active`.
- **fix(migration 0169)**: Production data on Railway included a `cc_buddies` row whose `status` was outside the original `('owned', 'shelter')` set, so re-adding the tightened `('owned', 'shelter', 'stored')` CHECK crashed every restart with `CheckViolationError`. Migration now `UPDATE`-normalises any NULL or out-of-set status to `'shelter'` before the DROP + re-ADD; safe no-op when the column is already clean.
- **New achievements + quests for buddy zones / storage / breeding / crafting specialties**: 11 new achievements covering Pack It Up (first buddy stored), Buddy Collector (10 stored at once), First Hatchling / Bonded Breeder (daycare collects), Habitat Hunter (5 different wild zones won), and Apprentice X / Renaissance Crafter for each crafting specialty. 5 new rotating quests covering daily store-one-buddy, weekly daycare collects (1 / 3), and daily/weekly specialty level-ups. New bus events `buddy_stored`, `daycare_egg_collected`, `specialty_level_up`, `wild_zone_visited` are subscribed by both `services/achievements.py` (with threshold checks for the count-based milestones) and `services/quests.py` (via the standard `_bumper` quest counter).
- **Unified staking UI**: New `core/framework/staking.py` shared `StakePanelView` provides the same Stake / Unstake / Claim / Refresh button shape and embed layout for every game's stake panel. Each game wires its own service callbacks via a `StakeAdapter`. `,craft stake` and `,farm stake` (with no args) now open the unified panel; `,buddy stake` / `,delve stake` / `,fish stake` keep their existing panels and can be migrated incrementally without breaking the text-arg path. Modal-driven amount entry with `all` / `max` shortcuts replaces the fragile text-arg flow when using buttons.
- **Crafting specialties**: Crafting now branches into five tracks -- Smithing, Alchemy, Cooking, Fletching, Tinkering. Every recipe declares one in `crafting_config.CRAFT_ITEMS`; a successful `,craft make` bumps both the aggregate `crafting_xp/level` AND the matching specialty `<spec>_xp / <spec>_level`. New `,craft specialties` command shows per-track progress; `,craft list <specialty>` filters by track; `,craft info` includes the specialty in its details panel. Migration `0171` adds the per-specialty xp/level columns to `user_crafting`.
- **Buddy daycare / breeding system**: New `,buddy daycare` group lets you deposit two of your owned buddies as parents (`,buddy daycare deposit <id1> <id2>`), pay a 1,000 BUD fee, wait 6 hours of incubation, then collect a pre-rolled egg (`,buddy daycare collect`) that lands in your held-egg slot and hatches the same way wild eggs do. Egg species is a 50/50 pick of the two parents' species; egg rarity tier rolls from a parent-tier-aware weight table (Legendary parents push Legendary children but never above the cap, Common parents can occasionally roll Uncommon kids). One slot per user per guild; `,buddy daycare cancel` abandons it without refunding the fee. Migration `0170` adds `cc_buddy_daycare`, and `services/fishing.give_held_egg` is the new shared helper any system can use to grant a held egg through the standard hatch pipeline.
- **Buddy storage ("computer")**: New `,buddy storage` (aliases `box`, `computer`, `pc`) opens a paginated view of buddies you've stashed away. `,buddy store <id>` moves an owned buddy into storage; `,buddy retrieve <id>` brings it back. Stored buddies don't count against the `MAX_OWNED_BUDDIES` cap, don't decay (the sweep already filters on `status='owned'` so stored rows naturally skip), and can't fight in arena / delve until withdrawn. Migration `0169` extends the `cc_buddies_status_chk` constraint to allow `'stored'` alongside `'owned'` / `'shelter'`. Storing your only buddy is blocked so the panel always has something to render.
- **Per-zone wild buddy spawns**: Wild-buddy spawns in fishing, farming, and the dungeon now pull from zone-specific species pools instead of one flat list. Fishing in the swamp hooks Shrek / Thornling types; the abyss spits Octopus / Wecco / Gloomer; farming the bog draws Shrek / Gloomer / Thornling; gold-tier delve floors get Draclet / Robo / Blazer. Adds `WILD_BUDDY_SPECIES_BY_ZONE` (fishing, farming) and `WILD_BUDDY_SPECIES_BY_THEME` (dungeon, keyed by floor theme: stone / silver / gold / boss) plus a `wild_buddy_species_pool()` resolver in each config. Falls back to the existing flat pools for any zone not listed so a future zone designer can ship the geography first and tune the pool later.
- **`,lb` consolidates every leaderboard under one command**: `,leaderboard` (alias `,lb`) now dispatches to every per-game leaderboard alongside the existing wealth / trading / staking categories. New game subcommands: `,lb buddy`, `,lb battles`, `,lb arena`, `,lb delve`, `,lb fish`, `,lb biggest`, `,lb farm`, `,lb craft`, `,lb achievements` (`,lb level` already worked). The per-cog forms (`,buddy lb`, `,fish lb`, `,delve lb`, etc.) are preserved as aliases so muscle memory keeps working. `,lb help` panel rebuilt with two grouped sections (Wealth + economy / Games + minigames).
- **Wild buddy battles in delves auto-continue the run**: After resolving a wild-buddy fight in `,delve`, the message handed off the same way `,delve next` does, so players can keep walking, fighting, mining, and looting from the same chat slot without typing `,delve next`. If the next room is another mob/boss/wild-battle the appropriate battle view is attached in place; empty / loot / shop / stairs rooms get the standard `_DelveRoomView`. If the run ended (death / completion) the result embed still shows with no view, mirroring legacy behaviour.
- **Forge Network + Crafting added to `,help currencies`**: The currency cheatsheet was missing a Forge Network section even though FORGE / INGOT / FGD have shipped, so newer players couldn't discover the `,craft` loop from `,help`. New "🔨 Forge Network" section explains FORGE (network coin, earn-only), INGOT (earn-only, minted by `,craft make`), and FGD (stablecoin, recipe fee). New "🔧 Crafting progression" section calls out the per-player Crafting level + per-specialty levels and points to `,help crafting` for the full lifecycle. Burn/Stake mechanics block now lists `,craft stake/claim` and FORGE in the cashout list. Quick-reference row gains `,help crafting`.

- **`,start` is now a real onboarding dashboard**: Was a static button-launcher hub; now reads your wallet, net worth, daily-claim status, and per-game progress (buddy / fishing / farming / delve / stones), then renders a **personalised "Next Steps"** list of 3-5 actions tuned to where you actually are. New players see a one-time **Starter Pack** button that atomically credits **$1,000 USD + 25 worm + 10 minnow bait + 10 wheat + 5 carrot seeds** so they can touch every game without grinding the faucet first. Buttons claim daily, hatch a buddy, cast your first line, plant your first crop, enter the dungeon, or jump to the multi-game hub via `,menu`. Migration `0168` adds `users.starter_pack_claimed_at` (idempotent flip-from-NULL grant). The old multi-game launcher is preserved as `,menu` (alias `,today`).
- **`,mylp` shows LP yield earned per position**: Per-row "Gain" used to read only swap-fee accrual via `lp_snapshot`, so a player whose pool had no swap volume saw "$0 over a week" even when the hourly LP-yield tick had been paying them. New `lp_positions.yield_paid_usd_raw` column (migration `0167`) is bumped on every successful per-position payout in `services/lp_yield.py`, the per-row gain breakdown now reads "fees $X + yield $Y", and the yield line shows "Earned so far: $Z" alongside the projected daily run-rate. Existing positions get a one-shot backfill that distributes lifetime LP_YIELD transactions evenly across the user's currently-active positions so the column starts non-zero on day one.
- **`,farm plant all <crop>` -- bulk-plant one crop**: Fill every empty plot with the same seed in a single command. Caps at `min(empty plots, seed packets)` so it never over-plants and never partially fails. Order-agnostic (`,farm plant all wheat` and `,farm plant wheat all` both work). Replies with the list of slots planted and the ready-by ETA.
- **Buddy stake accepts FREN, BBT, or `everything`**: `,buddy stake fren <amt|all>`, `,buddy stake bbt <amt|all>`, and `,buddy stake everything` all stake into the same BUD-yield clock. The accrual loop sums `fren_staked_raw + bbt_staked_raw` so both tokens drip BUD at the same per-day rate. `,buddy unstake fren|bbt|everything` mirrors the new shape and pays accrued BUD on the same call. Migration `0166` adds `bbt_staked_raw` on `user_buddy_economy`. `,buddy stake` (no args) shows a panel with separate FREN/BBT staked + available rows, USD context at live oracles, combined daily BUD rate, and the new command surface. Help and AI context for `,help bud` and `,help stones` updated to reflect the new shape and the per-stone currency layout.
- **Arena rewards rebalanced -- BBT is headline, BUD is a drip**: BBT was previously the small "universal battle token" while BUD did the heavy lifting; the ratio is now flipped. BBT pays base 25 + 2.5/level (cap 250) and BUD pays base 2.5 + 0.25/level (cap 25), so BBT is the dominant arena reward and BUD is a small drip to keep arena wired into the FREN-stake loop. Same multiplier stack applies to both (clean-fight bonus + tier multiplier).
- **Hashstone / Lockstone / Liqstone native currencies**: Each stone's `accepted_currencies` was narrowed so the stake currency reflects the stone's actual purpose -- Hashstone (PoW mining gear) takes BTC or SUN, Lockstone (PoS staking gear) takes DSC or ETH, Liqstone (LP gear, dollar-denominated) takes DSD or USDC. Migration `0165` rewrites every legacy DSD-staked row to the canonical first accepted symbol and rescales `staked_amount` via the per-guild oracle so `,inv`, `,bal`, and `,shop` stop saying "DSD staked" on every stone. Liqstone DSC/ETH legacy rows convert back to DSD with proper price-up.
- **Auto-levelup tries every accepted currency**: Previously the auto-levelup background task picked exactly the stored `lp_currency` and bailed if the player's balance was short, so a Hashstone bought in BTC silently stopped leveling the moment the player spent down their BTC even when they had plenty of SUN. Now the path tries the stored currency first and falls through every other entry in `accepted_currencies` (plus a legacy DSD/USDC tail for un-migrated stones), and stamps the actually-debited currency back onto `lp_currency` so subsequent ticks remember the new preference.
- **Crypt Tavern frame redrawn**: The "Surface Town" ASCII art was unreadable in Discord's font (slashes / underscores didn't line up). Replaced with a clean tavern facade frame -- "open for delvers" -- that renders correctly on both desktop and mobile clients.
- **LP bootstrap (pool seeder) incentive**: Empty / quiet pools now pay up to 5x base LP-yield APR to whoever seeds them, paid per-tick (not per-trade). The bonus decays on two axes -- TVL fully decays once the pool has $10,000 of liquidity, recent trade volume fully decays once $5,000 has rolled through. Both axes have to be in the bonus zone for the full multiplier, so a whaled-but-untraded pool stops paying once TVL fills up, and a quiet-but-deep pool stops paying once volume picks up. Recent volume decays -10% per tick, so once-busy pools that go quiet ease back into seeder bonus territory. Migration `0164` adds the `recent_volume_usd_raw` + `recent_volume_window_at` columns; `services/swap.py` bumps the counter on every swap; `services/lp_yield.py` reads it for the per-position multiplier and decays the column at end-of-tick.
- **Buddy arena pays BUD + BBT, never FREN**: The arena is the PvE BUD mint surface and the cross-game BBT mint surface; FREN stays on the buddy-interaction loop (talk / feed / pet drops) where it belongs. Resolves the wrong-token mint that shipped with the first arena cut. Migration `0163` renames `arena_fren_earned_raw -> arena_bud_earned_raw` so existing earnings carry forward; `,buddy arena` and `,buddy arena lb` panels now show BUD + BBT rewards with USD-equivalent at live oracles.
- **FREN drop on every buddy interaction (talk / feed / pet)**: The drop is now visible 100% of the time -- 50% lucky-drop at full payout, 50% tip drop at 10% payout. Amount still scales with buddy level + rarity tier + current happiness so a Lv30 Diamond at 100/100 happy pays substantially more than a Lv1 Common at 0/100. Each drop renders on its own line in the buddy panel with the FREN emoji, exact amount, and the buddy's level + happiness so the source is obvious.
- **Themed stones flip to native currency in `,inv` and `,bal`**: Tide / Heart / Crypt / Blood / Bloom / Vault stones bought before the per-stone `accepted_currencies` migration showed "DSD staked" because the legacy schema default never updated. Migration `0162` rewrites those rows to the canonical native currency (REEL / BUD / RUNE / BBT / HRV / USD respectively) and rescales `staked_amount` via the live per-guild oracle. Display fallback added to both inventory and bank balance: any future row whose `lp_currency` falls outside the stone's `accepted_currencies` tuple renders as the canonical first accepted currency, so inv / bal / shop never lie about the staking token.
- **Crypt Tavern delve panel rename**: `,delve` (no class) now shows "The Crypt Tavern -- Whispers from the Deep"; the post-class adventurer panel renders as "The Crypt Tavern -- {emoji} {name} the Lv{N} {Class}". The previous "X's Adventurer" embed was off-theme and read like a placeholder.
- **Forge Network + crafting minigame**: New earn-economy network introducing FORGE (network coin), FGD (stablecoin), and INGOT (earn-only token). The crafting cog (`,craft list/info/make/apply/bag/history/swap/cashout/stake/unstake/claim/lb`) consumes outputs from fishing (`fish_inventory`), farming (`crop_inventory`), and the dungeon (`copper/silver/gold_staked_raw`) and routes crafted items back into each game's existing inventory: bait into `user_fishing.bait_inventory`, fertilizer into `user_farming.fertilizer_inventory`, dungeon consumables into `user_dungeon.consumables`, and buddy treats applied directly to the active buddy. INGOT->FORGE and FORGE->USD reuse the shared `_price_impact` slippage formula via `services.fishing` helpers, so cashouts behave identically to the Lure / Crypt / Buddy / Harvest networks. Includes 21 starter recipes spanning all four games, INGOT staking with passive FORGE drip, net-worth integration (`crafting_stake_value` + `crafting_inventory_value`), and 8 achievements under the new `crafting` category.
- **BBT (Buddy Battle Token) cross-game battle currency**: Every wild battle in the bot -- fishing wild encounters, dungeon wild battles, farm wild battles, and buddy arena -- now mints BBT alongside the native game token. BBT is in `EARN_ONLY_TOKENS` and `BUD_SWAPPABLE_TOKENS`; it can only be earned through battle and only swapped through the Buddy Network burn-swap surface. Settings in `services/buddy_economy.py::mint_bbt_reward` apply the standard mint-impact oracle drop to keep chart parity with FREN, BUD, REEL, RUNE, and HRV.
- **Per-stone accepted currencies**: Each stone now has its own `accepted_currencies` tuple in `items_config.py` -- Hashstone takes BTC / SUN / DSD / USDC, Liqstone takes DSC / ETH / DSD / USDC, Vaultstone takes USD (bare wallet), Tidestone takes REEL, Heartstone takes BUD, Cryptstone takes RUNE, Bloodstone takes BBT, Bloomstone takes HRV. The shop buy + auto-levelup paths share a three-branch resolver (USD / stable / non-stable) that converts the cost via live oracle for non-stable tokens. Shop listings show per-stone accepted currencies inline.
- **Wild buddy battles in the dungeon**: Random wild encounters with rocky / physical / general-type CC buddies during a delve, mirroring the fishing / farm wild-battle pattern. Spawn -> stash on `user_dungeon` -> resolve via `buddy_battle.run_battle` -> mint RUNE + BBT and roll a capture chance. New `,delve battle` (aliases `fight_wild`, `wild`).
- **Wild buddy battles on the farm + harvest egg drops**: `,farm battle` (aliases `fight`, `wild`) handles spawned wild buddies (`wecco`, `shrek`, `donkey`, `cobble`, `fox`); harvests have a 2% egg-drop chance. Wins mint HRV + BBT and roll a capture chance.
- **`,me` showcase command**: 8-tab paginated player showcase covering overview / wallet / fishing / farming / dungeon / crafting / buddy / achievements. Net worth on the overview tab routes through `compute_net_worth` so the headline figure stays in lockstep with `,profile` and the leaderboards.
- **Group owner transfer with two-sided handshake**: New `,group transfer` subcommand suite (`propose`, `accept`, `decline`, `cancel`, `status`) -- the proposed owner must accept before ownership changes, with an explicit cancel path on either side. Stored in the `group_transfer_proposals` table.
- **Admin reports AI suite (`,admin reports ...`)**: Reports system now has end-to-end AI augmentation. `dump` ships a full untruncated markdown of every open report to your DMs. `diagnose <id>` runs the AI verifier (Ollama-first, OpenRouter fallback) and labels reports `real / spam / likely_fake / needs_more_info`. `autofix on/off/test/<id>` enqueues real reports for tier-A AI patch generation, opens a draft PR + GitHub issue, and DMs you the result. `auto-close on/off` rejects spam / likely_fake on classification. `close-old <days> [status]` bulk-closes stale reports. `queue scan/add/status/cancel/resume/clear` manages the autofix queue with `FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED` work-stealing semantics. Hard guardrails: `PATH_DENYLIST` blocks finance / migration / infra files, AST validation on patches, `MAX_DIFF_LINES = 250`, denied-pattern regex on added lines, never auto-merges -- always draft.

## [main] — 2026-04-24

### New Features
- **DiscoAI: memory + learning sidecar for the existing chat AI.** The self-hosted model experiment (numpy scratch transformer, HF pretrained backend, LoRA fine-tuner, torch/transformers/peft deps, custom orchestrator, PermissionError / torch / BatchEncoding / chat-template debugging spiral) is gone.  Generation stays where it's always been: the OpenRouter pipeline in `cogs/help.py`.  What DiscoAI ships instead: a thin `ai/` package with `MemoryService` (short-term Redis turns + long-term Postgres facts + episodic summaries), `ToolRegistry` with a default tool set over the Discoin FastAPI, and `TrainingLogger` that appends every `,ask` turn to `disco_training_turns` for later curation.  `cogs/help.py::ask_cmd` now asks the DiscoAI cog for `facts_for_prompt()` and splices remembered facts into the OpenRouter system prompt on every turn, so anything written via `,disco_remember` or `remember_fact` actually surfaces.  Admin commands: `,disco_forget`, `,disco_facts`, `,disco_remember`, `,disco_listen on|off`.  Migration 0123 (disco_facts / disco_episodes / disco_training_turns / disco_passive_channels) + export script (`python -m scripts.export_training_data`) stay; torch / transformers / peft / accelerate / safetensors / sentencepiece / tokenizers / numpy are removed from the dep tree; docker-entrypoint's HF HOME / usermod dance is gone.  Docs rewritten: `docs/dev-guide/discoai.md`.  12 tests in `tests/ai/` (down from 36 -- the inference / backend / orchestrator tests vanished with their subjects).

### Bug Fixes
- **Ollama native /api/chat fallback + vision-model for OpenRouter fallback + magic-byte MIME**: Real root cause of 'ai/ollama/vision HTTP 500 ... unsupported image' was a chain of three separate bugs.; 1. Hosted Ollama cloud rejects OpenAI-compat multimodal on several model routes (kimi-k2, qwen2-vl, most minicpm variants) with a generic HTTP 500. The OpenAI-compat shim can't translate {'type': 'image_url', 'image_url': {'url': data:...}} back into the native Ollama vision pipeline for those models, so the request dies before it ever reaches the model. This is a server-side shim gap, not a model-capability issue -- kimi CAN see images, just not when addressed that way.; Fix: complete_ollama_vision is now two-attempt. First tries OpenAI-compat /v1/chat/completions (still the happy path for local Ollama and some cloud models). On non-200 OR 200-with-empty-content, falls through to Ollama NATIVE /api/chat with the format Ollama's vision pipeline actually consumes: {'messages': [{'role': 'user', 'content': <prompt>, 'images': [<raw base64 without data: prefix>]}]}. Logs the OpenAI-compat failure reason AND announces the native retry so Railway logs make the handoff obvious. (`c8ef67dd`)
- **Diagnostic vision logging + stop AI from web-searching every reply**: Two reported issues.; Vision 500 debuggability (core/framework/ai/client.py + core/framework/agent_tools/tools/vision.py):; Ollama cloud returns an opaque HTTP 500 when the vision request targets a model that doesn't support images, when the image is too large for the account's tier, or when the model name is subtly wrong (kimi-k2 vs kimi-k2-vision, for example). The log line before this change only surfaced the HTTP status and response body, so Railway logs didn't tell ops which knob to turn. (`4b2f311d`)
- **Absorb heat kwarg on validator_reward bus + bump swap cap to $100M**: Two unrelated asks.; Bus kwarg crash (cogs/trades.py):; - cogs/stake.py started publishing 'validator_reward' with the new heat=heat_after field in commit 8b4704c. The subscriber Trades._on_validator_reward had only been updated for event_tag, so every tick now raises: (`00063927`)
- **Extend prompt-injection sanitizer to buddies, memory-refresh, and @everyone**: Buddies' and the main memory-refresh path were bypassing the AI safety helpers that handle_ai_reply / handle_ai_ambient already use. An attacker could lace ,buddy talk with injection payloads, poison cc_buddies.ai_memory, and the poisoned memory would feed straight back into every subsequent turn. Same story in the background _update_user_memory task -- user_msg / display_name / existing memory were spliced into a summarization prompt raw.; services/buddy_ai.py hardened:; - imports core.framework.ai.safety helpers (sanitize_input, sanitize_context_snippet, is_injection_attempt) (`d31e85f2`)
- **Sanitize web-search Sources so Discord invites and scam links stop rendering as citations**: Production bug report: the AI reply's 'Sources' button was rendering Discord invite redirects and literal pig-butchering scam pages as if they were genuine citations, because the list came straight from the data.web_search tool's SERP output with no filter.; Fix is a chokepoint sanitizer in cogs/help.py::_sanitize_source_entry. Every {title, url} pair routes through it before _SourcesView stores it, so even if the upstream backend ever gets replayed through another code path the filter still applies. Gates:; * URL scheme allowlist: only http/https. Kills javascript:, data:, discord:, steam:, mailto:, ftp:, file:. (`eabb5c42`)
- **Swallow 404 when battle-challenge message is gone at timeout**: Repro: user A challenges user B to a buddy battle, user B never clicks, the prompt ages out. The challenge view wakes, tries to edit the original message into a 'Challenge timed out' card, and the original is gone (user deleted it, mod cleaned the channel, or Discord's cache lapsed). Message.edit raises discord.NotFound (HTTP 404 / error code 10008 'Unknown Message'), the exception bubbles up through the command handler, and the bot posts the raw error embed in chat -- the 'lolol' the user flagged.; Fix: every terminal-state edit on challenge_msg (timeout / decline / aborted / result) is now wrapped so a missing message silently no-ops instead of leaking a 404 card. Four edit sites:; - Timeout, decline, and aborted paths share a nested _safe_edit helper that swallows discord.NotFound and logs.debug on any other HTTPException. (`494939f0`)
- **Uppercase wrapped symbols (MBTC/MSUN) + rescue stranded balances**: Root cause of 'swap group_token -> mBTC credited as MBTC in CeFi Other Network': Config.TOKENS used the mixed-case keys 'mBTC' and 'mSUN', but every write path in the codebase (update_wallet_holding, make_pool_id, the swap handler's .upper() on token_in/token_out, validators._exec_swap, _exec_send, etc.) forces UPPER on the symbol column. That left a three-way case mismatch:; * crypto_prices seeded with 'mBTC' (Config key verbatim); * wallet_holdings / pool rows written as 'MBTC' (write helpers uppercase) (`da474d1b`)
- **Sell-everything now eats slippage; swap-everything shows real batch cost**: Both 'everything' helpers under-priced vs. their single-token counterparts. Fixing the loopholes:; _sell_everything previously charged platform fee only. Single .sell applies platform fee AND price impact (a quadratic slippage term scaled by market cap), which meant users with whale-sized positions could dump bags at oracle spot via .sell everything instead of eating the real impact one symbol at a time. Rewrote:; - Preview computes per-token impact using the exact same formula as single .sell (trade.py:2289-2299): base = revenue / PRICE_IMPACT_DIVISOR, market-cap multiplier above 0.1% of mcap, capped at 0.95. Effective price = spot * (1 - impact). Revenue + fee are computed against eff_price, not spot. (`bbd14663`)
- **Route native<->group-token 404 to wrap/unwrap, not 'chain mine pool'**: Two bugs in the No-pool error path:; 1. The fallback hint told users to run '.chain mine pool', which is a MINING group subcommand (switches solo/pool/group mining) and has nothing to do with AMM pools. The right command to browse pools is .trade pool list. Replaced.; 2. The specific case that prompted this report -- 'BTC/GHO' -- is by design now: group tokens pair with mBTC on Moon Network, not raw BTC. Telling the user 'no pool exists' without explaining how to get there was useless. Added two smart branches: (`549f8651`)
- **Anchor mBTC/mSUN oracle to BTC/SUN within a 2% band**: Missed the basic peg mechanic on the first pass: mBTC and mSUN were configured with their own start_price and daily_vol and then left to GBM-drift independently of BTC / SUN. Over enough ticks the two would desync entirely, which is the whole reason a wrapped coin isn't a wrapped coin.; Fix:; - config.py mBTC / mSUN now declare peg_to (symbol of the underlying) and peg_band (max deviation fraction, 2%). daily_vol dropped to 1% so the chart stays smooth inside the band instead of sawtoothing at the clamp edges. (`183cc0db`)
- **Refund LP pro-rata before deleting stale group-token pools**: The original 0118 migration silently dropped lp_positions for every DSD/BTC/SUN pair, which would have wiped any user LP without a cent back. Fixed before anyone hits it.; Refund logic:; - For every lp_positions row whose pool is in the delete set, compute the user's pro-rata share of BOTH reserves via FLOOR(reserve * lp_shares / total_lp) in pure NUMERIC arithmetic so nothing drifts across the decimal boundary. (`56217ae0`)
- **$10k vault seed, MOON-pool backfill for existing groups, stake-list dropdown**: Three things:; Vault pool stops looking like dust:; - database/pools.py::create_vault_pool used to seed a 1-token position ('1 + ratio') which at typical token prices came out to ~42 cents total. Now seeds Config.GROUP_VAULT_POOL_SEED_USD ($10k default) per side at current oracle prices, so the treasury panel reads like real liquidity. Pool stays vault_locked -- players still can't swap against it, the reserves are just an accounting anchor for the mining vault. (`14d89bab`)
- **Lock bot to AI channels, kill $0 net-worth echo, seed group-token pools**: Addresses four user-reported issues:; Group tokens are tradeable immediately (no admin step needed):; - cogs/groups.py post-creation message no longer tells founders they need an admin to enable trading; migration 0106 already flipped the default and the UPDATE at line 735 sets trading_enabled=TRUE explicitly. The confusing text was the only barrier. (`7a612bbc`)

Wiring three concrete hooks off LP exposure to give them a real place in the loop, while keeping whale-farming defenses in place.; Mechanics:; - services/liquidity.py: group_token_symbols(gid) pulls the set of token_type='group' symbols from guild_tokens once; user_group_lp_value_usd(uid, gid) prices the user's pro-rata share of any pool where at least one side is a group token, in USD at live prices (same math as .mylp and net_worth.py). group_lp_work_bonus_pct(usd) applies a linear ramp (GROUP_LP_WORK_BONUS_PER_USD) with a hard cap (GROUP_LP_WORK_BONUS_CAP). (`87cffcaa`)
- **Opt-in time-lock tiers with Liqstone XP multiplier + early-unlock burn**: Pairing the new validator heat system on the staking side with a veCRV-flavored commitment mechanic on the LP side. Degens who actually stick around get paid; flaky ones pay to leave.; Mechanics:; - Three tiers picked per position: 7 days (1.5x XP), 30 days (2.5x XP), 90 days (4.0x XP). Multiplier applies to the Liqstone XP earned against that position during its lock window. Expired locks lapse implicitly with no DB write -- the tick just treats them as tier 0. (`6ab599a5`)

### Maintenance
- **Sanity-check sweep -- broaden user-token LP, harden writes, tests, help**: Second-pass audit of the branch:; Correctness:; - Broaden the LP hook from only token_type='group' to every guild_tokens row. - **Fix inflated staked_amount values via migration 0053**: Migration 0050 multiplied SUN-era staked values (e.g. 71,000) by 2x,; producing absurd amounts like 142,000. Reset all staked_amount to the; correct current DSD purchase prices: hashstone=7500, lockstone=6000, (`47bdf4ce`)
- **Guard migrations 0051 and 0052 against entrypoint race conditions**: 0051: Wrap RENAME COLUMN in DO $$ IF EXISTS block — entrypoint already; renames the column before the bot starts, so bare ALTER TABLE fails.; 0052: Remove bare BEGIN/COMMIT (fights migration runner's own transaction) (`a9f12b8f`)
- **Fix migration 0050: handle staked_sun OR staked_amount column name**: Entrypoint hotfix renames staked_sun->staked_amount before bot starts,; so migration 0050's stone rescale must work with either column name.; Use dynamic SQL (EXECUTE format) after checking which name exists. (`12b37176`)
- **Fix migration 0050: guard network column existence, fix DELETE alias syntax**: - Wrap wallet_holdings block in IF EXISTS column check (network col may not exist); - Wrap transactions block in IF EXISTS column check; - Remove 'AS old' alias from DELETE (invalid correlated alias syntax in PG) (`763ecf30`)
- **Fix migration 0050: merge duplicate wallet_holdings on discoin->dsc rename**: UniqueViolationError: user had both 'discoin' and 'dsc' DSD rows.; Merge strategy: add discoin amount into dsc row, delete discoin row,; then rename any remaining discoin rows with no dsc counterpart. (`3c542235`)
- **Guard stone table UPDATEs in migration 0050 against missing tables** (`92ef4de4`)

## [v1.7.2]  -  2026-04-06

### New Features

#### Economy Snapshot & Rollback System
- Added automatic economy snapshots every 30 minutes capturing balances, stones, and LP positions
- `.admin rollback` restores a guild's economy to any snapshot with full validation
- `.admin snapshots` lists available restore points with timestamps
- Configurable snapshot interval and retention count
- Snapshots include stone tables and LP positions to prevent double-spend on rollback
- Per-guild asyncio lock prevents concurrent restores
- Exclusive table locks during restore to close mid-rollback race conditions
- All restore values validated: negatives clamped to 0, NaN/null rejected before writes

#### Economy Rebalancing
- Nerfed income across work/beg/daily to slow inflation
- Fixed trade price exploit allowing arbitrage via stale cached prices
- Raised GDP scale floor to 15%; GDP scaling now shown in work output
- Added `.setjob` command for admins to assign user jobs; fixed setjob earnings calculation
- Fixed admin module bypass allowing non-admins to toggle economy modules
- `log_tx` now validates all amounts: rejects NaN/inf/negative, caps at 1 quadrillion

#### Admin Health Consolidation
- Consolidated `health`, `heal`, and `diag` under `.admin health` command group
- `.admin health check` -- full diagnostic report
- `.admin health heal` -- auto-detects issues and runs DB cleanup; each step guarded with try/except
- `.admin health cleanup` -- moved DB cleanup here from standalone command
- Removed orphaned `dev diag` and `admin diag` groups (were pure invoke redirects)
- Stripped redundant `manage_guild` guards from Health cog internal methods
- Updated dev status embed: GDP scale, rollback snapshots, DB counts; dropped noisy agent check

### Infrastructure
- Added 9 missing tables to schema.sql for fresh-install completeness
- Restored module-level imports deleted by sed cleanup (psutil, ErrorSource, Severity, datetime, heal_ai)

### Bug Fixes
- Fixed migration 0050: merge duplicate wallet_holdings on `discoin` -> `dsc` rename
- Fixed migration 0050: guard network column existence, fix DELETE alias syntax
- Fixed migration 0050: handle `staked_sun` OR `staked_amount` column name
- Guarded migrations 0051 and 0052 against entrypoint race conditions
- Fixed inflated `staked_amount` values via migration 0053
- Fixed chart tempfile import, `pvp_enabled` migration, missing mining columns
- Fixed epoch float `taken_at` in rollback and snapshots commands
- Fixed `float has no attr timestamp` for snapshot `taken_at` in dev status
- Fixed self-heal restarting idle loops that should not be auto-recovered
- Fixed `CommandRegistrationError` caused by duplicate admin health command registration
- Allowed `pvp off` during lock period -- only block re-enabling after exploit
