## [v1.7.0]  -  2026-04-06

### New Features

#### Exploit / PvP Heist System
- Added opt-in PvP economy game where players can attempt crypto heists against each other's wallets
- Three heist tiers (Exploit, Hack, Heist) with different success rates and payout multipliers  -  higher reward means higher risk
- Failure costs a penalty; success steals a portion of the target's wallet
- Defense shields: buy a 2-hour immunity window with `,defend`
- PvP is opt-in only  -  players must run `,pvp on` before they can be targeted or attack others
- **New commands**: `,exploit @target`, `,pvp [on|off]`, `,defend`, `,exploitstats [@user]`, `,exploithistory`
- **Smart PvP toggle lock:** Toggle is free (5s cooldown) until you trigger an exploit. The moment you run `,exploit` (win or lose), your toggle is locked for 1 hour  -  you can't turn PvP off to dodge retaliation. Lock timer shown in `,pvp` status.
- Crypto-themed flavor text for all outcomes (reentrancy guards, MEV bots, oracle failures, etc.)

#### Group Vault Tokens with PoW Network Binding
- Groups can now create persistent on-chain tokens bound to either the Sun Network or Bitcoin Network
- Token auto-created when a group founder sets a tag (`,group set tag=TAGNAME`)  -  symbol derived from the tag (up to 5 alphanumeric characters)
- Founders bind their token to a PoW network with `,group token network <sun|btc>` which locks both the token and an auto-created liquidity pool
- Per-block minting: every block mined by the group mints 1 token unit to the vault and adds liquidity to the LP pool
- Vault-locked LP: once bound, neither the token nor the LP can be traded, withdrawn, or modified  -  growth is purely through mining
- **New commands**: `,group token info`, `,group token network <sun|btc>`
- Includes 17 unit tests covering token derivation, symbol sanitization, and collision detection

#### Self-Healing Scheduler
- New background health system runs every 60 seconds and automatically recovers from:
  - Failed/stopped task loops across all cogs (cancel → sleep → restart pattern avoids race conditions)
  - Redis ghost connections where socket is hung but `is_connected` returns true (detected via periodic PING)
  - Circuit breaker: after 5 consecutive failures a loop enters degraded state and stops being auto-restarted
- Error channel notifications: loop restarts post amber embeds, circuit-breaker trips and Redis exhaustion send red embeds to all guild error channels
- Developer DMs: circuit-breaker trips and Redis retry exhaustion DM the configured `REPORT_TARGET_USER_ID`
- **New commands**: `,health notify [on|off]`  -  toggle notification delivery without stopping the scheduler
- **New commands**: `,health test [autofix]`  -  inject a simulated loop failure to verify self-heal works; `autofix` mode runs the heal immediately

#### AI Health Analysis
- `,health analyze` feeds the full diagnostic report to an AI backend and returns a plain-language breakdown with suggested fix steps
- Per-guild AI backend configuration: OpenRouter, Ollama, or global default
- Admin-only (requires Manage Server)
- `,admin ai heal [status|backend|model|baseurl|reset]`  -  configure per-guild AI provider for health analysis
- Integrates with tools.json surface area so users see a "Run Heal" button in AI responses

#### Stablecoin Shop Pricing
- All shop items (Hashstone, Lockstone, Vaultstone, Gambastone, Liqstone, Charm, Validator Guard) now accept stablecoin payment
- Prices denominated in USD with auto-conversion at current token prices
- `,shop buy <item> [amount] [currency]` accepts any configured stablecoin
- Sell back items for stablecoin refunds at current price
- API buy/sell endpoints wrapped in atomic PostgreSQL transactions with `ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING` to prevent race conditions

#### Slash Command Consolidation
- `/report` group: four separate slash commands merged into one group
  - `/report submit` (was `/report`), `/report browse` (was `/reports`), `/report claim` (was `/bugbounty`), `/report bounties` (was `/bounty list`)
  - Prefix aliases `,reports` and `,bugbounty` unchanged
- `/games` slash group organizes all play/gambling commands
- `/market` slash group organizes trading/economy commands

#### Guild Settings Auto-Seeding
- `guild_settings` rows are now automatically created for all guilds on bot ready and on new guild joins
- Prevents null reference errors for guilds that had never interacted with settings before

---

### Infrastructure & Deployment

#### Railway Postgres 18 / SSL Migration
- Full one-shot migration tool: set `RESTORE_FROM_EMBEDDED=1 CLEAN_RESTORE=1 FORCE_RESTORE=1` to migrate embedded PG17 data to Railway managed Postgres
- `CLEAN_RESTORE` now uses `DROP SCHEMA public CASCADE` + `CREATE SCHEMA public` for a guaranteed clean slate (previous per-table loop left sequences and caused duplicate key errors)
- `pg_restore --clean --if-exists` added as belt-and-suspenders
- PG17 and PG18 both installed in the image; version-auto-detected from data dir
- `DB_SSL_VERIFY=0` and `REDIS_SSL_VERIFY=0` are now Dockerfile defaults for Railway compatibility
- Redis `rediss://` scheme now properly handled in RedisBus (SSL connection pool)
- Entrypoint hotfixes now also apply missing `user_prefs` columns on every deploy

#### Security
- **CVE fix**: Bumped `path-to-regexp` to 8.4.2 (high + moderate DoS vulnerabilities via shadcn → msw chain)
- Removed `shadcn` from runtime dependencies (it's a CLI tool, not a runtime package)

---

### Bug Fixes
- Fixed `CommandRegistrationError` crash loop caused by conflicting `/games` and `/market` aliases
- Fixed slash command sync failure: truncated 8 docstrings exceeding Discord's 100-character limit
- Fixed admin AI heal crash: command group nesting was too deep, causing registration failure
- Fixed Redis SSL connection: wrong kwarg name in connection pool setup (`ssl_certreqs` → correct param)
- Fixed `pg_dump` version mismatch on backup: PG17 was left in PATH after restore, causing backups to fail against PG18 Railway server
- Fixed `muted_networks_*` and `pvp_enabled` columns missing from migrations  -  added as `0048_user_prefs_missing_columns.sql`
- Fixed FastAPI deprecation: `regex=` → `pattern=` in NFT query parameter
- Replaced all em-dashes, en-dashes, and Unicode minus signs project-wide for consistent terminal rendering

### Nightly 1.6.3 Fixes (included in this release)
- Stake farm 24h lock enforcement
- Leaderboard staked amount inclusion
- Airdrop/faucet `all` argument handling
- Swap everything NameError fix
- Stake lock reset on top-up
- Mining history population
- Chain mine symbol/emoji in history
- Fuzzy command suggestion ordering
- Wallet info optional address argument
- Dynamic `ctx.prefix` usage throughout

## [main]  -  2026-04-01

### Bug Fixes
- **Don't auto-delete messages that were false-positive command matches**: In bot channels (empty prefix), every message is tested against the; command list. If the first word happens to be a command name but the; rest of the message doesn't fit the command's arguments (TooManyArguments, (`e5740e2e`)
- **Remove duplicate oracle/MM infrastructure from cogs.crypto**: Both cogs.crypto and cogs.trade were running their own drift_task,; daily_reset_task, and _mm_trade_loop at the same PRICE_TICK_SECONDS; interval, each overwriting the other's price updates every tick. (`e102be95`)
- **Show vault fee in native coin instead of USD in swap embeds**: The confirmation and queued-swap embeds showed the vault contribution as; '≈ $0.0000 → USD', which is always $0.0000 for cheap coins like DSC; because the USD value of half the platform fee is sub-cent. (`8ebdf0d4`)
- **Pass pg_dump credentials via env vars and capture stdout errors**: pg_dump on some versions ignores passwords embedded in the connection URL;; passing PGHOST/PGPORT/PGUSER/PGPASSWORD as env vars is always reliable.; Also capture stdout alongside stderr in the error message  -  pg_dump writes (`282e3575`)
- **Unpack pow_mining_tick payouts by index instead of destructuring**: Payouts are 4- or 5-tuples (uid, earned, share_pct, user_hr, bonus_pct),; but the total_earned sum used `_, earned, _` which expects exactly 3 elements,; causing "too many values to unpack" on every PoW mining tick. (`e5dc04ac`)
- **Convert native coin to USD in deposit_to_vault for correct level progression**: Vault level thresholds are defined as cumulative USD values ($10, $50, ...).; Previously, vault deposits were stored in native coin amounts (BTC, ETH, DSC, SUN),; so for BTC the vault needed 10 BTC to hit level 1 instead of $10 worth of BTC. (`f52ec2b7`)
- **Atomic minting, DeFi-only transactions, command restructure**: - Fix mint_nft() call: remove invalid token_id kwarg, let DB assign atomically; - Fix buy_nft() call: pass price and currency args to match DB signature; - Restructure nft view: nft view SYMBOL for collection, nft view SYMBOL N for NFT (`7df75583`)

### Discord Bot
- **Fix swap platform fee: base on swap value, not gas fee; add vault deposit**: Three issues fixed:; 1. Platform fee was calculated as 10% of gas fee (tiny), now calculated; as 0.1% of swap value in gas coin terms (SWAP_PLATFORM_FEE_PCT). (`c31d2307`)
- **Add vault feed channel to admin setchannel command**: The vault_feed_channel was supported in the database layer and used by; the vault level-up announcement system, but was missing from the admin; setchannel UI. Admins can now use `/admin setchannel vault #channel` (`b6a34182`)
- **Fix help select menu exceeding 25-option Discord limit**: Merged the standalone vaults help category into the events category; to stay within Discord's 25-option select menu maximum (24 categories + Home). (`7a6b3ad5`)
- **Fix broken player commands, silent announce failures, and phase skipping**: Three bugs fixed:; 1. Command collision: The crypto cog registers aliases=["market"] on its; group, so the events cog's `market` hybrid group was shadowed and (`cb980651`)
- **Fix phase time display race condition in market status**: When a user queries /market status between tick cycles, the displayed; phase could show "0m 0s" remaining because the stored phase_index; hadn't been advanced yet. Added resolve_effective_phase() that (`1c02eee2`)
- **Make heartbeat monitoring interval-aware and harden drift tasks**: - heartbeat.py: Add register_interval() so each task declares its; expected cadence. stale_tasks() now uses interval×3 as the threshold; instead of a fixed 5min, so hourly tasks (backup, staking_tick, etc.) (`aa104a9d`)
- **Add time-aware task health indicators to diagnostics**: Task status now checks next_iteration vs expected interval instead of; just is_running/failed booleans:; - Green: running on schedule (`7b727a03`)
- **Wrap staking_tick loop body in try/except to prevent task death**: The staking_tick background task had no error handling around its; per-guild processing, so any exception would permanently kill the; task. Extracted the guild logic into _staking_tick_guild() and wrapped (`46f5e848`)
- **Fix airdrop command eating user funds when drop fails to spawn**: Money was deducted before calling _spawn_drop, which silently returned; if another drop was already active or if channel.send failed  -  leaving; the user with no drop and no funds. Now _spawn_drop returns a boolean, (`38a98799`)
- **Rebalance ape command to be -EV and add wallet drainer outcome**: The ape command was massively +EV (~1.82x), making it a money printer; when spammed. This rebalances it to ~0.72x EV (28% house edge) so it; loses money long-term while still having exciting big wins. (`5224f367`)
- **Remove cooldowns from dice and coinflip commands**: Removes the @user_cooldown(1) decorator from the dice, coinflip,; and their shortcode aliases (.dice, .cf, .flip). (`3f032690`)
- **Make beg a standalone prefix command instead of earn subcommand** (`4253918e`)
- **Fix missing game_lockout_until column and wrong holdings table name**: - Add migration 0025 to add game_lockout_until column to existing databases; (was only in schema.sql for fresh installs, never migrated to existing volumes); - Fix cogs/crypto.py and cogs/trade.py referencing non-existent "holdings" table (`b1382e11`)
- **Fix code review issues: market display, migration NOT NULL, docstring**: - Fix nft market showing internal DB ID instead of collection token_id; - Add token_id, token_hash, contract_address to get_listings() query; - Fix migration contract_address to include NOT NULL (match schema.sql) (`3eb63717`)

### Build
- **Fix Redis memory overcommit warning by disabling RDB persistence**: Redis warns about vm.overcommit_memory because it forks for background; saves (BGSAVE). Since Redis is used purely as an in-memory cache here,; disable RDB snapshots with --save "" in both the embedded (entrypoint) (`c6a828aa`)
- **Revert Dockerfile changes (VOLUME + pool seed default)**: Railway doesn't support VOLUME directive. Reverting all Dockerfile changes. (`badc8335`)
- **Disable SSL on embedded PostgreSQL to fix FATAL startup error**: The persistent volume's postgresql.conf has ssl=on from a prior config,; but the cert files at /var/lib/postgresql/data/certs/ don't exist in our; container. This causes a FATAL error that prevents PG from starting at all, (`a120f64a`)
- **Truncate old pg.log and suppress checkpoint noise in Railway**: - Truncate pg.log before PG startup to stop Railway replaying thousands; of historical error lines from the persistent volume on every deploy; - Set log_checkpoints=off and log_min_messages=warning to suppress (`aa09726a`)
- **Apply schema hotfixes in entrypoint before bot starts**: The migration system runs inside the Python bot process, but the; game_lockout_until errors fire immediately on first game interaction; before migrations may complete. Apply critical ALTER TABLE directly (`b8b14acb`)
- **Fix PostgreSQL failing to start in Railway containers**: Three issues addressed:; - Stale postmaster.pid from previous unclean shutdown prevents restart; - Missing container-friendly shared memory settings (dynamic_shared_memory_type=posix) (`f91aab2a`)
- **Revert last 3 docker commits**: Reverts:; - 2bbe1c1 Refactor entrypoint script for Discoin bot; - f3e538d Refactor Dockerfile stages and update dependencies (`ac4173c4`)
- **Refactor entrypoint script for Discoin bot** (`2bbe1c17`)
- **Refactor Dockerfile stages and update dependencies** (`f3e538d7`)
- **Disable embedded DB and Redis in docker-compose**: Disable embedded database and Redis in the container. (`ed426543`)

## [v1.5]  -  2026-03-31

### NFT Blockchain Overhaul
- **On-chain token hashes**: Every minted NFT now gets a unique SHA256 token hash for blockchain identity
- **Collection contract addresses**: Each NFT collection generates an ERC-721 contract address on deployment
- **Marketplace uses symbol+token_id**: `nft list`, `nft buy`, `nft unlist`, and `nft transfer` now require `<symbol> <token_id>` instead of ambiguous global IDs  -  prevents duplicate token ID issues across collections
- **Re-listing prevention**: Listing an already-listed NFT now updates the price with an "Updated" message instead of silently creating duplicates
- **Sale history command**: New `nft history <symbol> <token_id>` command shows the trade history of any NFT
- **Better error messages**: All NFT commands show clear usage examples when arguments are missing, instead of generic "argument is missing" errors
- **Fixed nft_sales table**: API queries now reference correct column names (`price` not `sale_price`, rarity via join not direct column)
- **Fixed API marketplace query**: Removed invalid `nl.active` column reference that caused 500 errors
- **New API endpoints**: Added `collection/{id}/sales` endpoint for collection sale history
- **Marketplace sorting**: API supports `sort=recent|price_asc|price_desc|rarity` and `rarity=` filter
- **Token hash display**: NFT view, mint, and history commands now show token hashes
- **Contract address display**: Collection views and NFT views show contract addresses

### Website NFT Marketplace
- **Full redesign**: OpenSea-inspired marketplace with rarity-colored borders and glow effects
- **Collection detail modals**: Click a collection to see all NFTs, floor price, total volume, mint progress
- **NFT detail modals**: Click any NFT to see full details with blockchain identity, sale history, contract info
- **Marketplace filters**: Sort by price, rarity, or recency; filter by rarity tier
- **Network badges**: ETH/DSC network badges on all NFT and collection cards
- **Token hash display**: Copyable token hashes and contract addresses throughout the UI
- **Listed status**: My NFTs tab shows which NFTs are currently listed on the marketplace
- **Responsive grid**: Optimized for mobile through desktop

### Database
- **Migration 0026**: Adds `contract_address` to `nft_collections`, `token_hash` to `nfts`, ensures `nft_sales` table exists in schema

---

## [v1.4]  -  2026-03-31

### NFT System
- **Atomic minting**: All minting operations use atomic transactions with proper rollback on failure
- **Sequential token IDs**: NFTs are assigned sequential token IDs within each collection
- **Network coin pricing**: Marketplace listings and sales use the network's native coin (ETH, DSC), not USD
- **Sales tracking**: NFT sales are tracked for collection and player statistics
- **Net worth inclusion**: NFT values are now included in net worth calculations
- **Unified view command**: `nft view <collection> [token_id]` replaces both `nft view <id>` and `nft collection <id>`
- **Removed `nft collection`**: Use `nft view <collection>` to view collection details instead
- **Added `nft collections`**: Lists all NFT collections on the server

### Predictions
- **Module toggle**: Admins can enable/disable predictions per server with `admin module predictions`
- **DM notifications**: Winners receive DM notifications when a market is resolved (requires `predictions` DMs enabled)

### Ape
- **Increased risk**: Rug rate increased to 85% (was 80%), break even reduced to 9%, moon reduced to 5%
- **Module toggle**: Admins can enable/disable ape per server with `admin module ape`

### Notifications
- **Removed ape toggle**: `notify ape` is no longer a notification category
- **Fixed defaults**: `dm_nft`, `dm_predictions`, and `dm_events` now correctly default to off

### Admin
- **Module toggles**: Added `admin module` toggles for: ape, nft, predictions, events, shop, games
- **NFT admin help**: Updated to show module toggle command

### Website
- **NFT gallery page**: Browse and view NFT collections and individual NFTs
- **Predictions page**: View and interact with prediction markets
- **Dashboard cards**: NFT and prediction summary cards on the main dashboard

### Technical
- All state-changing operations (minting, marketplace transactions, transfers) are now atomic with proper transaction guarantees

## [staged]  -  2026-03-30

### Admin Event Controls
- **`$admin event status`**: View current event, frequency settings, disabled events list, and module state in one dashboard.
- **`$admin event disable <type>`**: Block specific events from random triggers (e.g. `disable black_swan` to prevent catastrophic events). Admin can still trigger them manually.
- **`$admin event enable <type>`**: Re-enable disabled events. `disable all` / `enable all` for bulk control.
- **`$admin event frequency <preset|value>`**: Adjust random event trigger rate. Presets: `off`, `low` (~5h), `default` (~2h), `high` (~1h), `max` (~12min chaos mode). Custom float values accepted.
- **`$admin event list`**: Now shows 🚫 disabled badge next to disabled events.
- Random event engine now respects `module_events` toggle, `disabled_events` list, and per-guild `event_frequency`.

### Ape Command Improvements
- **Confirmation button**: Ape now shows a confirm/cancel prompt with full odds table and potential gains/losses before deducting funds. 30-second timeout auto-cancels.
- **Rebalanced payouts**: Legendary capped at 25-50x (was 160-300x). New **Ascended** tier at 0.01% chance for 80-100x payout.
- **5 outcome tiers**: Rugged (80%), Break Even (11.99%, 0.8-2x), Moon (7%, 10-25x), Legendary (1%, 25-50x), Ascended (0.01%, 80-100x).
- **`$ape` / `$degen` / `$yolo` top-level aliases**: No longer need to type `$earn ape`. All three work directly.
- **Job-scaled cost**: Entry cost now scales with job tier. Homeless: $20, Shitcoin Trencher: $100, Trader: $800, Exploiter: $12,500. Payouts scale proportionally.
- **DM notifications**: Moon+ wins DM'd to users with `$notify ape on`. Bus event `ape_completed` published for all outcomes.
- **Expanded flavor text**: 25 rug messages (was 15), 10 break-even (was 5), 13 moon (was 8), 7 legendary, 4 ascended.

### Notification Improvements
- **Market event DMs**: Users with `$notify events on` receive DM when a market event triggers (capped at 50 DMs per event).
- **Help updated**: Notification categories now list all 11 categories including events, ape, nft, and predictions with default states.

### Flavor Text Expansion
- **Daily rewards**: Now include random flavor text that varies by streak state (new streak, active streak, max streak).
- **Work**: 10 new cross-tier flavor messages added to the rotation.

### Status & Diagnostics Integration
- **Status page 2 (System Health)**: Market events system now shown with active event, remaining time, or idle/disabled state. Faucet loop added to monitored services.
- **Status page 3 (Economy Snapshot)**: Events config summary (module status, frequency, disabled count).
- **Dev status page 5 (Economy)**: Market events status with module/frequency/disabled/active event details.
- **`$dev check <system>`**: New command group for checking individual systems. Available: `events`, `mining`, `staking`, `validators`, `prices`, `savings`, `lending`, `security`, `faucet`, `chains`, `pools`, `errors`.
- **`$dev check events`**: Full events diagnostic  -  module status, frequency, active event details, disabled list, events channel, AI narration status.

### Dev Command Reorganization
- **Developer commands moved to `$dev`**: `log`, `errors` (summary/cmds/bot/export/clear), `diag` (health), `dbcleanup`  -  all now accessible via `$dev` in addition to `$admin`.
- **Admin help updated**: Diagnostics category now points to `$dev` for developer-focused commands.
- **Dev help expanded**: Full command listing with diagnostics, maintenance, and config sections.

### Help & Documentation Overhaul
- **New help category: Market Events** (`$help events`): Full event type table, commands, admin controls.
- **Updated help: Ape section**: Reflects job-scaled costs with tier table, updated payout ratios.
- **Updated help overview**: Added "Events & Degen" section with `$event`, `$ape` commands.
- **Updated getting started**: Events category listed in help categories.
- **Updated admin help**: New "Events" admin category with full disable/enable/frequency/status docs.
- **Updated admin help: Channels & Modules**: Added events, nft, predictions, ape feed channels.
- **Bot channel prefix fix**: Guild prefix (e.g. `$`) now works in bot channels alongside bare commands. Previously only `,` and no-prefix worked.

### Player Token & NFT Deployment
- **`$token deploy`**: Protocol Dev+ players can deploy custom ERC-20 tokens on PoS networks (ETH/DSC) with burn rates, transfer fees, max supply. Charges deployment gas. Auto-seeds liquidity pool. Token appears in `$crypto`.
- **`$token info`**: View any token's on-chain contract details (burn rate, fees, deployer).
- **`$nft deploy`**: Protocol Dev+ players can deploy ERC-721 NFT collections on PoS networks. Charges deployment gas. Mint price denominated in network's native coin.
- **NFT gas fees**: Minting, buying, and transferring NFTs now charge gas in the network's native coin.
- **`$nft view`**: Full-size NFT images in embeds (was thumbnail). Shows on-chain contract details.
- **Token contract enforcement**: Buy/sell now apply `burn_rate` (tokens destroyed, supply reduced) and `transfer_fee` (routed to community reserves) from on-chain contracts.

### New Command: .ape (Degen Mode)
- **`$ape`** / `$degen` / `$yolo`: Spend $50 to ape into a random shitcoin. 80% rugged (lose $50), 12% break even ($50-150), 7% moon ($2k-$8k), 1% legendary ($8k-$15k).
- Themed messages: rug pulls, honeypots, 100x gems, fake audits.
- ~2.5 min cooldown. Wins posted to ape feed channel.

### Market Events System
- **12 event types**: bull_run, bear_market, fed_rate_hike/cut, black_swan, whale_pump, rug_pull, pandemic, regulation, adoption, etf_approved, exchange_hack.
- Events modify price **volatility** and add **directional bias** to the GBM drift.
- Random trigger ~once per 2 hours. Auto-expire after duration.
- **Player commands**: `$event` (view current), `$event list` (all types).
- **Admin commands**: `$admin event trigger <type>`, `$admin event clear`, `$admin event list`.
- Events announced in the events feed channel.

### Economy Rebalance
- **Daily reward**: $200 → **$500** base (streaks/job perks still stack).
- **Starting balance**: $100 → **$20** for new players. Existing balances unchanged.

### Critical Bug Fixes
- **Swap "all" gas overdraw**: Users were losing their full balance when `$swap ETH USDC all` tried to send full balance + gas from the same wallet. Now reserves gas from swap amount. Same fix for `$trade pool add all`.
- **Prediction bet datetime crash**: `'>=' not supported between datetime and float`  -  fixed comparison with DB-coerced epoch floats.
- **Prediction bet "all"**: `$predict bet 1 YES all` now bets full wallet.
- **Reports browse crash**: `'float' has no attribute 'timestamp'`  -  missing `hasattr()` guard.
- **`$admin setchannel all`**: `faucet_channel` was missing from DB allowlist.
- **`$dev config interval`**: "Task is already launched" error  -  properly checks running state before restart.

### NFT Marketplace Hardening
- Buy command charges gas + has try/except rollback on payment failure.
- Transfer command charges gas.
- Prediction resolve/cancel handle individual payout errors gracefully.
- Prediction bets re-check balance and market status after confirmation.

### Feed Channels & Module Toggles
- **New feed channels**: nft, predictions, events, ape.
- **New module toggles**: ape, nft, predictions, events (all on by default).
- **Channel categories**: economy, earning, fun, bot, collectibles  -  batch-set feeds.
- **DM notifications**: events, nft, predictions, ape categories added (default OFF).

### UX Improvements
- **Cooldowns are not errors**: Amber ⏳ notice instead of red ❌. Auto-deletes after cooldown.
- **Error buttons**: BadArgument errors show Report Bug + Help buttons with command hints.
- **Cooldowns halved**: Global 0.5x multiplier on all cooldowns.
- **Security thresholds doubled**: Gambling velocity 50→100, command flood 30→60, identical command 15→30.
- **`$dev config dm on|off`**: Toggle auto-DM reports.
- **`$dev config channel on|off`**: Toggle channel error posting.
- **`$report-edit`**: Documented in help (was implemented but hidden).

### Documentation
- New: `docs/user-guide/nfts.md`, `docs/user-guide/predictions.md`.
- Updated: `docs/user-guide/defi.md` (pool syntax), `docs/user-guide/trading.md` (pool reference), `docs/user-guide/economy.md` (daily/ape/events), `docs/admin-guide/commands.md` (all new commands/feeds/modules).
- Admin help: Added "NFTs & Predictions" and "Market Events" categories.
- AI command reference: All new commands documented for Disco assistant.

### Bot Channel Mode (No-Prefix)
- **`.admin botchannel #channel`**: Toggle no-prefix mode for a channel. Players type bare commands (`work`, `buy 10 eth`, `help`)  -  no prefix needed.
- If a player accidentally uses a prefix (e.g. `,work`) in a bot channel, the bot hints: "No prefix needed in this channel  -  just type `work`".
- Run `.admin botchannel` with no arguments to list current bot channels.
- Stored as comma-separated channel IDs in `guild_settings.bot_channels`.

### Unified Configuration Source of Truth
- **New `constants/` package**: Pure Python modules with zero framework imports. Every business constant now lives in exactly one canonical place. Six domain modules: `validators.py`, `trading.py`, `economy.py`, `security.py`, `games.py`, `ui.py`.
- **PoS validator constants consolidated**: 20 constants (VALIDATOR_TICK, VALIDATOR_REWARD, TREASURY_CUT, MAX_SLASH_COUNT, SLASH_RATE, GAS_TIERS, etc.) moved from duplicated definitions in `cogs/validators.py`, `cogs/stake.py`, `core/framework/ui.py`, `cogs/bank.py`, `cogs/trades.py` into `constants/validators.py`.
- **Trading constants consolidated**: DEFAULT_SWAP_FEE, PLATFORM_FEE_RATIO, SLIPPAGE_WARN, PRICE_FLOOR, USD/TOKEN_PRECISION, etc. moved from `services/swap.py`, `cogs/trade.py`, `api/v2/routers/trading.py` into `constants/trading.py`.
- **Economy constants consolidated**: 31 constants (CHAIN_SWITCH_COOLDOWN, STAKE_LOCK_PERIOD, MIN_COLLATERAL_RATIO, AI_COOLDOWN_SECS, etc.) into `constants/economy.py`.
- **Security constants bridged**: `constants/security.py` re-exports from `security/config.py`, so `cogs/economy_security.py` now respects `SEC_*` env overrides for the first time.
- **UI color constants**: 13 embed colors moved to `constants/ui.py`, re-exported by `core/framework/ui.py` for backward compatibility.
- **Game constants**: Mines, slots, and anti-bot thresholds in `constants/games.py`.
- **AST-based regression test** (`tests/test_constants_single_source.py`): Scans all cogs/, services/, api/, core/framework/ files for duplicate constant definitions. Prevents re-introducing duplicates.
- **API endpoint** `GET /api/v2/constants`: Exposes validators, trading, games, and economy constants to the frontend.
- **Frontend hook** `useConstants()`: React hook fetching shared constants from the API.

### User Display Fixes
- **`mention()` helper usage**: `cogs/report.py` and `core/framework/internal_commands.py` now use the `mention()` helper instead of raw `<@user_id>` strings.
- **`UserLink` component**: `frontend/app/dashboard/staking/page.tsx` and `admin/page.tsx` now use `<UserLink>` instead of raw user IDs.

### Help Embed Fix
- **Fixed double-prefix bug**: The `_fix_prefix()` function in `cogs/help.py` had a catch-all replacement that caused `.n ` to become `.n n ` in all help commands. Removed the redundant line.

### Mining Reliability Fixes
- **mining_tick now has error handling**: Added try/except with full logging (was silently crashing on any exception). Added heartbeat pulse for health tracking.
- **Reward credit failures now logged**: The `_credit()` inner function was swallowing all exceptions with bare `pass`. Now logs both fallback attempts with user/guild/amount details.
- **Invalid rig IDs now logged**: Rigs with IDs not in `Config.MINING_RIGS` were silently skipped. Now warns with the unknown IDs so stale data can be identified.
- **Zero hashrate early return now logged**: When no valid rigs are active, the debug log captures it instead of silently returning.

### Bot Health & Status System
- **Heartbeat registry** (`core/framework/heartbeat.py`): In-memory task loop health tracking. Each background task calls `pulse()` on every iteration. `stale_tasks()` detects loops that stopped firing.
- **12 task loops instrumented**: mining_tick, chain_tick, keeper_loop, price_drift, price_drift_trade, staking_tick, validator_tick, pos_validator_tick, savings_interest, loan_interest, security_scan, faucet, hourly_summary, backup.
- **`.status` command**: Player-facing service health display. Shows green/yellow/red per system with verifiable proof (last block, sample price, validator count, tick ages). No sensitive data.
- **`.dev` command group**: Developer-only commands restricted to `REPORT_TARGET_USER_ID`.
  - `.dev status`  -  comprehensive diagnostic DM with memory, latency, heartbeats, full diagnostic results
  - `.dev heartbeat`  -  live task loop heartbeat display
  - `.dev config interval <hours>`  -  set auto-DM interval
- **Auto status DM**: Bot DMs the developer a status summary every 4 hours (configurable via `DEV_STATUS_DM_INTERVAL` env var or `.dev config interval`).

### Documentation Overhaul
- **Merged changelogs**: Combined `CLEANUP_CHANGELOG.md` into `CHANGELOG.md`.
- **Configuration docs rewritten**: `docs/getting-started/configuration.md` now documents the full layered config system (constants/, config.py, .env, security/config.py) with complete constant tables.
- **Docs theme updated**: Replaced amber/deep-orange with deep purple palette. Removed GitHub repo link from docs site.
- **Orphaned docs deleted**: Removed 4 duplicate/stale files (`docs/API.md`, `docs/CONFIGURATION.md`, `docs/INTERNAL_COMMANDS.md`, `docs/contributing.md`).

- **Remove all scattered permission checks  -  single auth gate via JWT**: - Remove every redundant is_owner/is_bot_manager/is_admin check from; endpoint handlers in permissions.py and security.py. require_admin; is the single gate  -  if you passed it, you have access. (`68403b39`)
- **Unify auth: resolve bot_manager permissions at login, not per-request**: - Bot manager check now happens in the auth router (guild select +; token refresh) and is baked into the JWT as is_owner + is_admin; - require_admin no longer queries the DB  -  just reads JWT claims (`7663adc7`)
- **Grant bot_manager full owner+admin permissions across all endpoints**: Bot manager now gets is_owner=True and is_admin=True in both; require_admin and require_security_access, so they pass every; permission check without needing per-endpoint bot_manager gates. (`3b340f13`)

- **Exempt admins from security locks, clear all locks on first startup**: - bot check (cogs/security.py): users with the administrator Discord; permission now bypass enforcement the same way the guild owner does; - API middleware: requests carrying an admin JWT claim skip all (`27ab06cc`)
- **Add .admin refresh and .admin reset group with updated help** (`a03e3ccc`)

### Bug Fixes
- **Move faucet migration into database/migrations so it runs on startup**: The migration was placed in migrations/ (root) instead of database/migrations/; where _run_migrations() scans, so module_faucet was never added to existing; guild_settings tables. (`3fd5d1ac`)
- **Prevent http:// mixed-content redirects in groups and pools routers**: When FastAPI's Starlette is behind an SSL-terminating proxy, its default; trailing-slash redirect generates Location: http:// URLs, causing browser; mixed-content blocks. Setting redirect_slashes=False on the affected routers (`c37eaab4`)
- **Define missing hasPendingChanges variable in admin page**: The variable was referenced in the JSX but never declared. Added a; derived boolean from localEdits and pendingResets state. (`f4a577e4`)
- **Update CI workflow to trigger on main and copilot/** branches** (`6ea358cd`)
- **Charts ts→time, volume tracking, profile userId guard, CORS PUT**: Charts:; - CandleData schema: rename ts (ISO string) → time (Unix int seconds); - market.py get_candles: return int(r["bucket"].timestamp()) for time (`ded22aeb`)
- **Auth state lost on hard page refresh / direct URL navigation**: The Zustand auth store initialized with token=null on every page load.; hydrate() was only called from useAuth(), which was never used in the; admin page or dashboard layout, so the store never got populated from (`f5dbe738`)
- **Create reports/bounties tables via migration + fix timestamp crash**: Root cause 1  -  missing migration; Reports and bounties were only defined in schema.sql (fresh-install; only). Existing databases never had the tables or columns created, so (`11d11d61`)
- **Multiply all shop and group upgrade prices by 1000**: SUN was priced 1000x too low relative to the crypto market. All; cost_sun values in SHOP_ITEMS and GROUP_UPGRADES (both legacy and V2; tiered) are multiplied by 1000 to reflect correct valuations. (`705ea2c4`)

### Changes
- **Initial plan** (`a2699b3c`)

## [nightly]  -  2026-03-23

### Unified AMM Pricing for Buy/Sell
- **`buy_token()` and `sell_token()` now use AMM pool pricing** when a USD-TOKEN liquidity pool exists with active liquidity, eliminating the arbitrage gap between `/buy`+`/sell` (fixed oracle price) and `/swap` (AMM price).
- **Oracle fallback preserved**: tokens without a liquidity pool continue to use the `crypto_prices.price` oracle, so existing tokens without pools are unaffected.
- **Pool reserves updated atomically**: when AMM pricing is used, pool reserves are updated inside the same DB transaction as the balance changes, keeping the pool and price in sync.
- **Oracle price synced to AMM spot price**: after each AMM-priced trade, `crypto_prices.price` is updated to the new post-trade spot price, keeping the oracle consistent with the pool.
- **Liquidity validation**: buy orders that would exceed available pool token reserves, and sell orders that would exceed pool USD reserves, are rejected with a clear error message.

### Mining Endpoints Auth Fix
- **Removed `guild_id` query parameter** from 6 mining endpoints (`/networks`, `/networks/{symbol}`, `/miners`, `/groups`, `/groups/{group_id}`, `/blocks`)  -  they now derive `guild_id` from the authenticated user via `get_current_user`, matching every other endpoint in the API. This fixes the 422 validation error the frontend was hitting.
- **Added `to_iso()` wrapping** for `last_block_ts` and `block_ts` timestamp fields returned by mining endpoints, and updated the corresponding Pydantic schema fields from `datetime | None` to `str | None` for consistency with the rest of the API.

### Question Detection → Help Redirect
- **New `_detect_help_question()` method** on `PromptInterpreter`: detects natural-language questions (e.g. "how do I stake my ETH?", "where can I buy tokens?", "help me with mining") using a compiled regex and redirects them to the relevant help category instead of trying to execute an action.
- **Class-level constants**: `_QUESTION_RE` regex pattern covering "how do I", "how to", "how can I", "where do I", "what is the command for", "help me with", "I need help with" patterns; `_HELP_KEYWORD_MAP` mapping 50+ action keywords to 12 help categories (staking, economy, trading, mining, lending, pools, wallet, earn, games, chain, validators, shop).
- **Integrated early in `_parse_rule_based()`**: question detection runs before direct aliases and action matching, ensuring questions never accidentally trigger commands.
- **Removed old handler**: the previous "how do I send/transfer/pay" handler (which incorrectly executed `cmd_send`) has been removed  -  now covered by the general question detector.

---

## [nightly]  -  2026-03-22

### Internal Commands Expansion
- **30+ new replay command registrations**: admin, earn, mine (rigs/status/network), ask, tx, delegate/undelegate, stake subcommands (list/mine/validator list/stats/delegations/networks/mempool), pool list, contract list, bank savings/loan, admin settings/listtokens/listnetworks/blockstatus/reports/halt list.
- **18 new direct aliases**: `admin`, `earn`, `mine`, `mining`, `rigs`, `crypto`, `airdrop`, `drop`, `ask`, `loan`, `savings`, `rates`, `explorer`, `tx`, `mempool`, `delegate`, `undelegate`.
- **15 native internal commands** (no prefix equivalent):
  - `top_gainers` / `top_losers`  -  tokens by 24h price change
  - `market_overview`  -  aggregate market stats (avg change, top gainer/loser)
  - `compare_tokens`  -  side-by-side token comparison (`bot ETH vs BTC`)
  - `token_holders`  -  top holders of a token (`bot SUN whales`)
  - `server_stats`  -  economy overview (users, USD, treasury, miners, stakers)
  - `treasury_balance`  -  guild treasury balance
  - `explorer_summary`  -  chain explorer summary
  - `network_list` / `network_info`  -  blockchain network details
  - `gas_fees`  -  current gas fee per network
  - `admin_audit_log`  -  recent admin action history (manage_guild required)
- **50+ natural-language regex patterns** added to `_parse_rule_based()` covering: economy ("my net worth", "my savings"), staking ("my stakes", "my delegations"), mining ("my rigs", "mining stats"), markets ("top gainers", "ETH vs BTC", "SUN whales"), pools ("show pools"), leaderboards ("who's the richest"), chain ("explorer", "tx lookup"), admin ("server settings", "halted networks", "admin audit log"), gambling ("coinflip 100", "slots 50"), rates ("savings rates", "gas fees"), and network ("show networks", "ethereum network info", "show contracts").
- **13 new multi-prompt aliases** for LLM catalog enrichment.
- **Rewritten `command_help` embed** with 12 organized categories (Economy, Trading, Market Intel, Mining, Staking, Pools, Chain, Gambling, Shop, Server, Utility, Admin).
- **Fixed `_InteractionBackedMessage`**: added `_state`, `id`, `mentions`, and `reply()` method so slash-command replay doesn't crash with "has no attribute _state".
- **New documentation**: `docs/INTERNAL_COMMANDS.md`  -  full reference for all NL commands, indexing system, and how to add new commands.
- **Auto-generated docs page at `/docs`**: dark-themed HTML page listing all prefix commands (from cogs) and all internal NL commands (from registry) with parameters, examples, domains, and permission badges. Swagger API docs moved from `/docs` to `/docs/api`.

## [released]  -  2026-03-22 (patch 2.2)

### Help Embed Updates
- **Mining help renamed**: "SUN Mining" → "PoW Mining" with new BTC chain field (₿ 6.25 BTC reward, 2016-block retarget), `.mine assign` command with examples, chain assignment explanation, and corrected rig hashrate stats matching actual config.
- **Gambling stats**: added `.play stats` / `.gambstats` command to gambling help.
- **Work GDP scaling**: added GDP-scaled earnings and per-tier daily work cap note to Daily & Work help.

### Staking Feed Embeds  -  NODE → FARM
- **Feed embeds no longer leak into user's channel**: removed `channel=ctx.channel` from stake/unstake event publishes. Users now only see the "Staked/Unstaked Successfully" reply; the detailed feed embed goes only to the configured staking feed channel.
- **Renamed all feed embed titles**: NODE DEPOSIT → FARM DEPOSIT, NODE WITHDRAWAL → FARM WITHDRAWAL, NODE SLASH → FARM SLASH, NODE REWARD → FARM REWARD.
- **Renamed all "Node" fields → "Farm"** in feed embeds and DM slash notifications.
- **"Depositors" → "Stakers"** in slash and reward feed embeds.
- **AI slash prompt** updated to farm terminology.
- **Footer** "Hourly node yield" → "Hourly farm yield".

### Airdrop Prefix Fix
- **Prefix `.airdrop` now works**: was failing silently because `ephemeral=True` is not supported on prefix commands. Slash commands still get ephemeral; prefix commands now use `delete_after=5`.

## [released]  -  2026-03-22 (patch 2.1)

### Sunstone → Hashstone Rename
- **Sunstone renamed to Hashstone** across the entire codebase  -  items config, all cogs, database, API, frontend. Hashstone XP is now earned via PoW mining (was confusingly named after SUN).

### Modular PoW Mining
- **`Config.POW_NETWORKS`** dict for modular PoW chain config; legacy `SUN_MINE`/`BTC_MINE`/`MINE_CONFIGS` kept as aliases.
- **New DB tables**: `pow_network_state` + `rig_chain_assignments` with one-time migrations from old tables.
- **Mining tick rewrite**: loops all `POW_NETWORKS`; unified `_process_pow_guild` dispatches to chain-specific logic (full SUN logic or proportional distribution for BTC/others).
- **`.mine assign`** now accepts any PoW network symbol, not just BTC/SUN.
- **Hashstone XP** granted in all PoW chains proportional to miner hashrate share.

### BTC Mining
- Players can assign rigs to mine BTC or SUN independently.
- Separate BTC network state with difficulty retarget.
- `btc_quantity` column on `mining_rigs`, `mining_network_btc` table.

### Economic Balance Controls
- **GDP-scaled work income**: work earnings scale down as total server wealth grows (floor: 10% of listed range).
- **Per-tier daily work caps**: prevents session-grinding abuse ($5k/day for Homeless → $20M/day for Exploiter).
- `get_work_today()` DB method for efficient daily earnings lookup.

### Compact Embeds & Confirmations
- Removed 61 blank spacer fields and 19 `.blank()` calls across all cogs.
- Converted 15 single-line non-inline fields to `inline=True` (3 per row).
- **Confirmation dialogs** added for: bank deposit, bank withdraw, savings deposit/withdraw (USD and SUN). All confirmations use `ConfirmView` with 30s timeout, author-locked, edited in-place.

### AI & Security Hardening
- Injection-proof prompt handling, 25/hr AI quota, output sanitization, retry on delivery failure.
- **Net worth**: shared `services/net_worth.py` for consistent Discord/dashboard calculation.

### Admin & Reports
- Paginated `CategoryPaginator` for admin help.
- **Permission commands**: `.admin perm add/remove/clear/list` for role-based command permissions.
- **Report tags**: 10-tag system, admin-to-reporter DM messaging, `ReportTagSelect` UI.
- Fix admin reports 1024-char field limit with `_dm_reports_paginated` helper.

### Gambling Stats
- `get_gambling_stats()` DB method, API endpoint, `.gambstats` command.

### Validator Fixes
- Fix `.vals` 400 error and 25-field embed limit (chunk 3 per page).

### XP Bug Fixes
- **Vaultstone/Lockstone XP at zero balance**: replaced `XP_SCALE_MIN` floor (0.1) with 0.0 and added `amount > 0` guards in bank.py and stake.py. No more phantom XP from empty positions.

### Help Text Consistency
- **Command references updated**: help embed, overview, and AI prompts now use current `/stake` command names (`.stake list`, `.stake farm`, `.stake unstake`, `.stake mine`) instead of legacy `.nodelist`, `.node`, `.unnode`, `.mynodes`.
- **Validator commands updated**: help now shows `.stake validator register/list/stats/networks/mempool/delegate/undelegate/delegations` instead of standalone `.vregister`, `.vals`, etc.
- **"Yield nodes" → "yield farms"** throughout all help text to match actual code terminology.

## [released]  -  2026-03-21 (patch 2)

### Backup Management
- **`.backup delete <filename>`**  -  delete a specific backup file (aliases: `rm`, `del`)
- **`.backup clear [keep=1]`**  -  delete all old backups, keeping the N most recent (aliases: `prune`, `cleanup`)
- **API endpoints**: `POST /api/v1/admin/backup/delete` (body: `{filename}`) and `POST /api/v1/admin/backup/clear` (body: `{keep: N}`)
- Path traversal protection on delete (rejects `..`, `/`, `\` in filename)

### Charting Overhaul
- **5 technical indicators**: Volume bars, EMA 20, SMA 50, Bollinger Bands (20,2), RSI (14) with synced sub-chart
- **Indicator toggle buttons** with tooltips below the chart controls
- **All 11 networks** in the Prices page filter bar
- **Shared theme colors**  -  removed inline DARK/LIGHT from Prices.js
- **Removed SUNCOPE** references from chart command help text
- **Network column** added to gainers/losers table
- **Card hover animations** on token selector

## [released]  -  2026-03-21 (patch 1)

### Dashboard  -  Open to All Users
- **Auth overhaul**: Any Discord server member can now log in to the dashboard (not just admins). Admin panel remains hidden from non-admins; all admin endpoints enforce `is_admin` server-side.
- **Optional TOTP 2FA**: Users can enable two-factor authentication from the dashboard via the shield icon. QR code setup flow with authenticator app support. 2FA challenge screen on login when enabled.
- **User info**: Avatar and username displayed in sidebar. JWT now carries avatar claim.
- **Updated text**: Auth and guild picker screens updated for non-admin users.

### Dashboard  -  Interactive Trading
- **5 service modules** extracted from Discord cogs into shared `services/` layer (no Discord dependencies):
  - `services/trade.py`  -  buy/sell tokens
  - `services/stake.py`  -  stake/unstake on validators
  - `services/liquidity.py`  -  add/remove LP
  - `services/transfer.py`  -  send USD to other users
  - `services/savings.py`  -  deposit/withdraw savings
- **11 new API endpoints** under `/api/v1/me/*` with JWT auth and 3-second rate limiting:
  - `POST /me/buy`, `/me/sell`, `/me/stake`, `/me/unstake`
  - `POST /me/lp/add`, `/me/lp/remove`, `/me/transfer`
  - `POST /me/savings/deposit`, `/me/savings/withdraw`
  - `GET /me/stakes`, `/me/savings`
- **5 interactive modals**: TradeModal (buy/sell), StakeModal, LiquidityModal, TransferModal, SavingsModal  -  wired into Validators, Pools, Savings, Portfolio, and Prices pages.

### Dashboard  -  Admin Overhaul
- **Admin.js split**: 1,900-line monolith decomposed into 14 sub-components under `components/admin/` (AdminComponents, AISection, DangerZone, + 11 section stubs).
- **DangerZone**: Server reset and economy reset now require typing exact confirmation text.
- **New command**: `.admin reseteconomy`  -  resets user data (balances, holdings, items, stakes) but keeps pools, validators, tokens, and settings intact.

### Dashboard  -  Design System
- **Shared theme**: `theme/colors.js`  -  consolidated DARK/LIGHT color palettes, `useColors()` hook, design tokens (radius, transitions, fonts).
- **Animations**: `theme/animations.css`  -  fadeSlideUp, scaleIn, shimmer, pulseGlow keyframes + utility classes.
- **System theme**: Respects `prefers-color-scheme` when no explicit preference saved. Live listener for system theme changes.
- **Smooth transitions**: CSS transition on background-color, color, border-color for theme switching.

### Dashboard  -  Mobile & UX
- **Bottom navigation**: Fixed bottom bar on mobile (Portfolio, Swap, Home, Explorer) with Discord-style active indicator.
- **Page transitions**: fadeSlideUp animation on page mount.
- **Notification system**: Global toast notifications via `NotificationContext` (showSuccess, showError, showInfo).
- **Loading skeletons**: Content-shaped shimmer loaders (CardSkeleton, TableRowSkeleton, StatSkeleton, PageSkeleton).
- **ResponsiveTable**: Component that renders as MUI Table on desktop, stacked cards on mobile.
- **ConfirmDialog**: Reusable confirmation dialog with optional typed confirmation and danger mode.

### Dashboard  -  Security
- **Audit log table**: `audit_log` in schema.sql for tracking admin actions.
- **JWT secret warning**: Startup warning if `JWT_SECRET` is still the default value.
- **2FA database**: `user_2fa` table for TOTP secrets.

### Networks  -  Expansion to 10
- **Added Bitcoin Network** (PoW, mineable): BTC, WBTC, STX, ORDI, SATS, RUNE, BADGER, RIF, ALEX. Buy/sell only  -  no AMM pools.
- **Added Avalanche Network** (PoS): AVAX + 10 ecosystem tokens (JOE, GMX, QI, PNG, COQ, etc.) + AUSD stablecoin + 5 validators.
- **Added Polygon Network** (PoS): POL + 11 ecosystem tokens (QUICK, GHST, SAND, SUSHI, GNS, etc.) + PUSD stablecoin + 5 validators.
- **Added Cosmos Network** (PoS): ATOM + 11 ecosystem tokens (OSMO, INJ, TIA, DYDX, SEI, AKT, etc.) + CUSD stablecoin + 5 validators.
- **Added Sui Network** (PoS): SUI + 10 ecosystem tokens (DEEP, NAVX, CETUS, TURBOS, SCALLOP, etc.) + SUIUSD stablecoin + 5 validators.
- **Added Aptos Network** (PoS): APT + 8 ecosystem tokens (GUI, THL, TORTUGA, DITTO, etc.) + APUSD stablecoin + 5 validators.
- **Added Near Network** (PoS): NEAR + 8 ecosystem tokens (REF, AURORA_N, BRRR, LINEAR, etc.) + NUSD stablecoin + 5 validators.
- **Removed Arbitrum/Optimism as separate networks**: ARB and OP moved to Ethereum as regular (non-stakeable) tokens. L2-specific tokens and stablecoins (ARUSD, OPUSD) removed.
- **Sun Network expanded**: Added themed tokens (LUMEN, FLARE, HELIOS, AURORA, CORONA, NOVA, SOLARI, PHOTON, ZENITH) + SNUSD stablecoin.
- **BTC mining config**: `BTC_MINE` added with 6.25 BTC block reward, 2016-block difficulty retarget, higher initial difficulty than SUN.

### Discord Bot
- **Help info tab**: New "Info" category in `.help` dropdown showing dashboard URL, server count, uptime, latency, and config summary.
- **Bot start time**: `_start_time` tracked on bot init for uptime display.

### Security & Reliability
- **Full atomicity**: All service modules (trade, stake, savings, liquidity) now wrap multi-step DB operations in `async with db.atomic():`  -  BEGIN IMMEDIATE / COMMIT with automatic ROLLBACK on any exception. No more partial state on failures.
- **Critical bug fix**: Price impact check in trade.py moved BEFORE execution  -  previously a >50% impact rejection happened after wallet was already debited, causing silent fund loss.
- **TOTP timing attack**: `_verify_totp()` no longer early-returns on first match  -  iterates all time windows to prevent timing side-channel.
- **2FA replay prevention**: `tfa_pending` JWTs are single-use (tracked in `_used_2fa_tokens` set). Max 5 attempts per token before lockout.
- **Amount validation**: All `/me/*` endpoints now reject NaN, Infinity, and non-finite amounts via `math.isfinite()`.
- **Rate limit race fix**: `_rate_check()` sets timestamp BEFORE checking cooldown to close TOCTOU race window.
- **LP minting guard**: Rejects zero-reserve pools and zero-LP-token mints to prevent division-by-zero exploits.

### Legacy Cleanup
- **Network mappings updated**: All 8 cog files updated with full 11-network mappings. Removed Arbitrum/Optimism network references. Added Bitcoin, Avalanche, Polygon, Cosmos, Sui, Aptos, Near to all `_NET_SHORT`, `_NET_ALIASES`, and `INITIAL_BASE_GAS` dicts.
- **Duplicate code removed**: Deleted duplicate `_NETWORK_SHORTS` and `_NET_NATIVE` definitions in `cogs/bank.py`.
- **Schema consolidated**: Added 6 missing CREATE TABLE statements to `schema.sql` (wallet_holdings, lockstones, vaultstones, charm_inventory, active_charms, pos_delegations).

### Documentation
- **README.md**: Updated network list (11 networks), token count (120+), feature list (dashboard, 2FA, interactive trading), command table. Added note that ARB/OP are Ethereum tokens, not separate networks.
- **CHANGELOG.md**: Created (this file).
- **.env.example, Dockerfile, docker-compose.yml**: Verified up-to-date, no changes needed.

### Bug Fixes
- **Reset server**: Now includes shop items (sunstones, lockstones, vaultstones, charms), savings deposits, SUN loans, and PoS delegations.
- **Price seeding, pool seeding, validator seeding**: All dynamic from `Config.TOKENS` / `Config.VALIDATORS`  -  new networks auto-seed on startup.
- **Bitcoin pools**: BTC ecosystem tokens are buy/sell only (no AMM pools)  -  matches Bitcoin's real-world nature.

### Removed
- `.rep` command and reputation field from profile embed.
- Profile customization commands (`.profile setbio`, `.profile settitle`, `.profile setcolor`, `.profile setbanner`).
- Custom profile title, bio, color, banner from balance/profile display  -  now uses Discoin branding.
- Arbitrum Network and Optimism Network as separate chains (ARB/OP remain as Ethereum tokens).

### Token Totals
- **11 networks**: Sun (PoW), Bitcoin (PoW), Ethereum, Solana, BNB, Avalanche, Polygon, Cosmos, Sui, Aptos, Near
- **~120+ tokens** with real 2026 crypto prices
- **50+ validators** across all PoS networks
- **11 stablecoins** (one per network, except Bitcoin which uses BTCUSD)
